organisés  à  Taghit  (W.  de  Bechar)  en  décembre  2014,  avec  le  soutien  du 
Ministère de la Culture et de l'Office National des Droits d'Auteur et droits 
voisins (ONDA). 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Cet ouvrage a été traduit de l'arabe ("ﺔﻠﻛﺂﺘﳌا عﻼﻘﻟا" Editions Barzakh, Alger,

Mohamed Sari.

Mohamed SARI 

Tiɣermin yettmmeččen 

Ungal 

Tasuqelt ɣer tmaziɣt sɣur : 
Habib-Allah MANSOURI 

Editions 
Voir par le Savoir 

 

 
 
 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 

 

 
 
 

 
 
 

 
 
  Ẓẓleɣ ɣef umeṭreḥ, ttxemmimeɣ kan amek ad xedmeɣ 
akken  ad  iyi-tawi  tnafa,  ad  ṭṭseɣ  yiwen  n  yiḍes  d  aẓayan 
ara  iyi-yesrewlen  seg  uḥebber  ɣef  yifasuten  n  usarag  n 
ustan  i  yi-yettraǧun  azekka.  Hatan  yewweḍ-d  lawan  n 
tbeddi deg uxxam n teɣdemt. Nekk, ɛerqent-iyi irkelli, ur 
ẓriɣ  ara  acu  i  ilaq  ad  xedmeɣ.  Awezlu  yewɛer,  lexyuḍ-is 
mcubbaken  mačči  d  kra.  D  lbumba  yendin,  nettraǧu  kan 
melmi ad teṭṭerḍeq seg teswiɛt ɣer tayeḍ. Yernu ẓriɣ, ulac 
ccek  deg  waya,  ulac  win  ara  s-imenɛen.  Ad  yester  Rebbi 
tameddit,  wa  ad  yessebɛed  fell-aneɣ  tabuciḍant-agi  ara 
yeglun  s  uzegzaw  d  uquran.  Aɣezzan  ibedd  ɣef  yiri  n 
lerwaḥ  yenḥaren,  ireɛɛeḍ,  yessḥillef  fell-aneɣ ;  times-ines 
tebda tettaweḍ ɣer wudmawen. Ur umineɣ ara tella yiwet 
n  lqeḍra  i  izemren  ad  t-yerren  ɣer  lḥedd-is  neɣ  ad  as-
tekkes  seg  uqerruy-is  tikti-nni  n  ucɛal  n  tmes  deg  yal 
taɣmert  n  tmurt.  Anagar  asfel  i  izemren  ad  as-yekkes 
urfan wa ad t-yesserked. Zik-nni, d tikci n yiwet n teqcict 
tahuskayt,  d  taḥurrit  d  asfel  iɛumm.  Maca  tura,  tarkeft  n 
teqcicin 
tiḥurriyin  akked  yiqenṭaren  n 
yidinaren,  n  yidularen  neɣ  n  yuru  ur  zmiren  ara  ad  rren 
algam  i  uɣersiw-agi,  win  i  ibedden  ɣef  yiɣurab  n  deffir, 
ara  aɣ-yesbelɛen.  Itteffeɣ-d  yiwen  n  ssut  i  d-yekkan  seg 

tihuskayin, 

 

- 1 - 

 
 
- 7 - 

 

daxel-iw,  yeqqar-iyi-d  ljerḥ-a  yessaḍen  tuget  n  lejwareḥ. 
Aṭṭan-a,  anagar  agzam,    ur  yesɛi  ddwa  ḥellu.  Ussan-a 
weɛrit  mačči  d  kra,  ulac  win  ara  s-imenɛen,  ḥala  win 
iwumi s-tedɛa yemma-s s teɣzi n laɛmer, am wakken i yi-
d-teqqar  yemma,  ad  fell-as  yeɛfu,  yerḥem,  asmi  i  yi-d-
tettmeslay  ɣef  yiwen  n  ṭṭraḍ  niḍen,  ar  tura  urǧin  ḥlan 
lejruḥ-is. 
Suffɣeɣ-d  iɣmisen  i  d-yeqqimen  s  ṭul  n  wass  deg 
 
uqrab-iw  mebla  ma  ufiɣ  ula  d  yiwet  n  ddqiqa  akken  ad 
ten-nwaliɣ  ulamma  d  awali,  bdiɣ  qqareɣ  deg-sen  armi  i 
yi-yesduqqes  ssut  n  tilifun,  ad  as-tiniḍ  d  tuqqsa  n  tsafut. 
Acu yebɣa ɣur-i umseḍḍeɛ-agi deg tlemmast n yiḍ ? Ahat 
d  anemhal  n  uɣmis,  yebɣa  ad  iẓer  ma  beddlen  azemz  n 
uzmaz ?  Neɣ  ahat  d  yemma-s  n  umeḥbus ?  Ala,  truḥ-d 
ɣur-i ass-a ɣer tnarit-inu. Teccekta-yi-d i tikkelt niḍen ɣef 
yir  liḥala  ideg  tettidir,  am  wakken  tessuter  deg-i  ad 
xedmeɣ  iwumi  zemreɣ  iwakken  ad  smenɛeɣ  mmi-s  seg 
bu-yikurdan, 
tessider 
aqerruy-is seg  leḥya d lqella  n  tezmert-ines. Sdat n tegnit 
yecban ta, ur ufiɣ ara acu ad as-iniɣ anagar kra n wawalen 
d  tenfaliyin  i  d-yeffɣen  seg  wul-iw  akken  ad  tt-heddneɣ, 
xas akken ẓriɣ  awezlu-agi yewɛer mačči d kra. Beddeɣ s 
tmara,  aqerruy-iw  yeḥjeb-it  usigna  n  kra  n  teqbucin  n 
lbirra  i  swiɣ  akked  yiwet  n  terbaɛt  i  imenɛen  seg 
tmesɣanit yemmɣen ɣef tmurt iseggasen-a ineggura. 
  Deg tezwara, iban-iyi-d ssut-nni am wakken yettergigi, 
yettnegzam,  ur  yemmid  ara  maḍi.  D  ssut  n  yiwen  i  yi-

sakin  xenqen-tt  yimeṭṭawen, 

 
 
- 8 - 

 

yessnen mliḥ, imi s yisem-iw i yi-yessawal, maca d ssut n 
umdan i yeččan tiyita, win iɣef teɣli twaɣit. 
Mmi…  Nabil,  mmi…  a  gma  Ɛebdelqader…  tselleḍ-iyi  … 
tegziḍ d acu i ak-d-qqareɣ… 
  Zrint  kra  n  tsinin,  sakin    ɛeqleɣ  anwa-t  bab  n  ssut-agi 
iwumi yeffeɣ laɛqel. 
Mmi… la ak-d-qqareɣ mmi… la iyi-tselleḍ ? nufa-t yeččur 
d idammen… 
  Yessusem ubabat, dayen yeffeɣ-it laɛqel, ur yezmir ad 
yenṭeq  ula  s  yiwen  n  wawal.  Teɣli-d  gar-aneɣ  yiwet  n 
tsusmi d taẓayant, tesxelxel-iyi mliḥ, teɛreq-iyi tririt. Ula d 
nekk nnejlan fell-i wawalen, ur ufiɣ ara acu ad d-iniɣ sdat 
n  tmettant  n  mmi-s  n  umeddakkel-iw  yeɛzizen  fell-i.  D 
Nabil i yemmuten, d yir lmut, wagi dayen iḍehren. Ssneɣ 
Racid Benɣusa ugar n kraḍet n tmerwin n yiseggasen aya, 
seg  wussan  n  usileɣ  deg  uɣerbaz  n  yiselmaden.  Ddunit, 
urǧin tella ḥninet fell-as, ur t-tezgil ara, ula netta seg tama-
s  yesɣaray  aqerruy-is  dayen  kan,  ur  yettaǧǧa  ara  tardest 
neɣ imi n wuccay, ɣas meẓẓiyet, seg yizerfan-is igamanen. 
Yernu,  ulac  win  i  izemren,  ɣas  meqqer  ccan-is,  ad  as-
yessenɣes  seg-sen  ulamma  tarebbɛet  n  umilimetr.  Ma 
yewweḍ ad yeṭṭenṭen akka, almi qessiḥet tiyita i yečča. 
Ur  ak-itteffeɣ  ara  laɛqel  ay  ameddakkel-iw,  ahat  d  ljerḥ 
kan i yettwajreḥ, dɣa yeɣli, yefsex… 
Ala… ala… d tarsast… sliɣ i ssut-is seg uxxam… d tarsast 
n tmeẓyant, mačči d tiyita n ujenwi neɣ n uɛekkaz. 
Srugemteɣ : « tarsast  n  tmeẓyant ».  Imir-n  kan  ulɣent 
 
deg  uqerruy-iw  tiwlifin,  am  wakken  d  asaru  amsaltan  i 

 
 
- 9 - 

 

ttwaliɣ.  Aneḍlib  yebɣa  ad  ineɣ  baba-s,  maca  tarsast  tḥuz 
mmi-s. Iban aṭas-aya segmi t-yettgabar, tuɣ-it yeffer deffir 
n  tewwurt  n  uɣerbaz  alemmas,  mi  iruḥ  Nabil  ad  yeldi 
tawwurt n umraḥ, imi ulac laman, s leqfel i tt-ɣellqen tura, 
teḍra  twaɣit,  maca  mačči  am  wakken  i  as-yenwa  uneḍlib 
deg  tazwara.  Amek  i  yemneɛ  Racid ?  Ayɣer  d  mmi-s  i 
yeččan tiyita ? Ineḍliben-agi, uɣen tannumi ur zegglen ara 
iswan-nsen. D turdiwin-agi i yezzin deg wallaɣ-iw, mi lliɣ 
ttlusuɣ lqecc-iw s temɣawla akken ad laḥqeɣ ameddakkel-
iw, mi sliɣ i tenfalit « tarsast n tmeẓyant ». 
  Lḥiɣ  s  temɣawla  deg  tlemmast  n  yixxamen  ijdiden 
yeṭṭsen  deg  tsusmi  d  ṭṭlam.  Leḥyuḍ-nsen  mazal-iten  s 
ssiman,  amur  ameqqran  deg-sen  ad  qqimen  d  tinmeslin 
kan,  acku  iban  urǧin  ad  yekfu  lebni-nni.  Iberdan,  yečča-
ten  uɣebbar,  deg  yal  tama  ad  ak-mmagren  arrumen  n 
lebni  yettuṭeggren  sya  u  sya.  Lḥemdullah,  aseggas-a 
ageffur  iɛeṭṭel.  Yiwen  n  wass  kan  n  ugeffur,  ad  uɣalen 
yiberdan  d  ibrunen  n  waluḍ,  ulac  tikli  deg-sen,  ad 
ttwareglen irkelli. Deg umkan ad aɣ-yeffeɣ laɛqel, neɣ ad 
neḥzen mi iɛeṭṭel ugeffur, nuɣal nferreḥ mi ad nwali tesḥa 
tegnawt,  nessaram  ad  iɛeṭṭel  uɣurar.  Am  wakken  i  d-
yeqqar  umeddakkel-iw  Racid  s  usqecmeɛ :  acu  ara 
nexdem s ugeffur ? Isaffen-nneɣ smarayen aman-nsen deg 
lebḥur, neɣ itess-iten yijdi. Akal, ttun-t medden, yeqqim d 
asuki,  ulac  win  ara  t-ixedmen.  Lbaṭaṭa  d  yirden,  nettawi-
ten-id  seg  tmurt  n  Kanada.  Ayɣer  ur  nessutur  ara  deg 
Wanẓar  ad  yesmir  i  yicercuren  n  ugeffur  ɣef  wakal  n 
tmurt  n  Kanada.  Akka  ulac  acu  ara  naggad  ɣef  rrezq  d 

 
 
- 10 - 

 

nneɛma-nneɣ. D tidet, tikwal yettaḍsa umdan seg lehmum 
d twuɣa i d-ɣellin fell-as. 
  Asedeger  gar  uxxam-iw  d  uɣerbaz  alemmas  « Ibn 
Badis »  ur  yewwiḍ  ara  sin  n  yikilumitren.Yenɣa-yi 
uḥebber,  yenneqbaḍ  wul-iw.  Ttɛeddayent  sdat  n  wallen-
iw tiwelfin n twaɣit am wakken i tt-sugneɣ, dɣa ad ɣiwleɣ 
ad  tent-snefleɣ  s  tiyaḍ  ara  silɣeɣ  imir-n  kan.  Asugen-inu 
suguneɣ-d  mmi-s  n 
yezzuɣur-it  usirem-inu,  dɣa 
umeddakkel-iw  d  ajraḥ  kan  i  yejreḥ,  mazal-it  yedder, 
yettarra  nnefs.  Mačči  kan  akka,  ttwaliɣ-t  yeẓẓel  ɣef 
umeṭreḥ  deg  ssbiṭar,  cudden-as  akk  ideddicen-is,  ula  d 
amejjay yettezmumug, yumer mliḥ mi yessemneɛ yiwen n 
yilemẓi seg tmettant. 
  Amraḥ n uɣerbaz alemmas yezdel fell-as ṭṭlam, yewɛer 
ad  tɛeqleḍ  udmawen  n  kra  n  wid  d-yusan.  Amkan-a 
ssneɣ-t mliḥ, ur cukkeɣ ara yella acu i ibeddlen deg-s, ɣas 
ma yella aṭas aya ur d-zziɣ ara ɣer da. Zegreɣ tawwurt n  
lemraḥ,  allen-iw  ttqellibent  kan  ɣef  teɣtest.  Sellmeɣ  ɣef 
wid  yellan  din.  Rran-iyi-d  s  usrugmet,  ur  tfehmeḍ  tigert 
deg yimeslayen-nni. Teɣli-d ɣef umkan d yimdanen yellan 
din yiwet n tsusmi d taẓayant, tegzem-iyi awal, tesgugem-
iyi.  Yernu  d  acu  lfayda  n  yimeslayen  sdat  n  tmettant ? 
Rriḥa-ines  tergel  inzaren,  tettarra  algam  i  yilsawen. 
Ḥebseɣ, walaɣ sya u sya. Walaɣ Racid yeqqim ɣef tmurt, 
isenned  ɣef  aɣrab,  aqerruy-is  gar  yifassen-is.  Tameṭṭut-is, 
Nasira,  ur  tebɛid  ara  fell-as,  teqqim  ddaw  n  tesqift  n 
tnawalt i tnewwer yiwet n teftilt, tettru s tsusmi, mebla ma 
yuli-as yiwen n wawal. Ruḥeɣ ɣer umeddakkel-iw, serseɣ 

 
 
- 11 - 

 

afus-iw  ɣef  tayet-is.  Yerfed  uqerruy-is  s  laɛqel  kan, 
imuqel-iyi-d  s  yiwet  n  tmuɣli  yexsin,  war  tudert,  mebla 
ma  yenṭeq  ula  s  yiwen  n  wawal.  Imir-n  kan  i  faqeɣ 
yemmut  mmi-s.  Xemmemeɣ  ad  t-sebbreɣ  s  kra  n 
tenfaliyin  timasɣanin  i  nessexdam  deg  tegnatin  yecban 
tigi, am teflest n uneslem s lajel d ssber. Maca ẓriɣ amek i 
yettxemmim Racid d tgensas-ines ɣef temsal-agi, ɣef waya 
ttiɣ-tent deg yimi-w, sbelɛeɣ-tent sakin. 
  Beddeɣ deg umkan-iw kan, teɛreq-iyi cedd n uyeddid, 
ur  ẓriɣ  ara  acu  i  ilaq  ad  xedmeɣ  sdat  n  twuɣa  am  tagi. 
Lḥiɣ  sakin  ɣer  umkan  ideg  teḍra  tmenɣiwt.  Sin  n 
yemsulta bedden tama n tfekka yeẓẓlen ɣef tmurt, ur ǧǧin 
ḥedd ad iqerreb ɣur-s.  
  Tikkelt  taneggarut  ideg  walaɣ  deg-s  Nabil,  zrin  fell-as 
semmus  n  yiseggasen  aya,  asmi  i  yi-yeɛreḍ  baba-s  akken 
ad  sweɣ  lqehwa  akked  terbaɛt  n  yimeddukkal  almend  n 
usmures-ines  deg  ukayad  n  lbak.  Tafekka-nni  yeẓẓlen 
sdat-i  ur  tettemcabi  ara  maḍi  ɣer  tugna-nni  iressan  deg 
wallaɣ-iw.  Wagi  yellan  sdat-i  ur  yemxalaf  ara  ɣef  tugna 
tamatut  n  yimeɣnasen  n  yimusa  ineslemẓra  imṭurfa : 
aččamar  ameqqran  yečča  udem-is,  aqerru  iseṭṭel  akked 
tqendurt taɣezfant i ttlusun deg tmurt n Afɣanistan, yerra 
nnig-s  abalṭu  n  uglim  aberkan,  deg  yiḍarren-is  tayuga  n 
yirkassen n waddal, d iberkanen ula d nitni. Imuyag-ines 
d  imeqqranen,  banen-d  mliḥ,  iban  yeḍɛef  mliḥ  ɣef  zik. 
Walaɣ  afus-is  ayeffus  yetti  ddaw  n  tmessaḍt,  iban-iyi-d 
am  wakken  yella  acu  yeffer.  Bɣiɣ  ad  waliɣ  s  wallen-iw, 

 
 
- 12 - 

 

unzeɣ  ɣur-s  ciṭuḥ,  maca  ibedd  yiwen  n  umsaltu  deg 
ubrid-iw : 
—Sani  tleḥḥuḍ  akka  a  Si  Muḥemmed…  ulac  win  ara 
iqerrben ɣur-s… ulac win ara inalen tafekka n lmegget. 
Ɣas  akken  ɛeqleɣ  d  acu-tt  tɣawsa-nni  taberkant.  D 
 
tameẓyant tatumatikt. D acu-t uhdum-a ? D  acu  txeddem 
tmeẓyant deg ufus n teɣtest ? Anwa i iqersen ihi ? 
Seqsaɣ  amsaltu  ɣef  tmeẓyant.  Yečča-yi  s  wallen,  am 
 
wakken yebɣa ad iyi-yini ur ggar ara iman-ik deg wayen i 
k-yexḍan. Ɛerḍeɣ ad as-sfehmeɣ ur lliɣ ara d aberrani ɣef 
twacult. Ilemẓi-nni yeẓẓlen sdat-neɣ d mmi-s n uḥbib-iw, 
tili  ur  iyi-yessawal  ara  deg  tlemmast  n  yiḍ.  Lehdur-iw 
sqelqen-t, yerra-yi-d s wurfan : 
Nniɣ-ak-d yegdel a Si… 
—Ɛebdelqader  Bensedduq…  Amastan  ɣer  tsenbaḍt,  d 
ameddakkel n Si Aḥmed, akumisar n temsulta. 
  Yennecraḥ  wudem  n  umsaltu,  sakin  yečča-yi  s  wallen 
ɣas akken  tetwelles  liḥala.  Ahat  d aqelleb i  yettqellib deg 
ccfawat-ines  limmer  ad  d-yaf  yiwet  n  tugna  n  yiwen  n 
umastan yettakken anzi ɣur-i i d-yemlal deg tgennariyin n 
uxxam n teɣdemt. 
  Kra  n  lweqt  umbaɛd,  yenṭeq-d  ɣur-i  s  yiwet  n  taɣect 
ḥninet ciṭuḥ : 
—D  tidet,  d  tameẓyant  i  yeṭṭef  yilemẓi-agi  deg  ufus-is 
ayeffus. Yettbin-d am wakken d tinɣiman. Maca ur nezmir 
ara  ad  nefru  tamsalt-a  seg  tura.  Ɣef  temgarḍt-is  d 
yidmaren-is  idammen  gersen,  ɣummen  adeddic.  Ḥala 
tasleḍt  n  tfekka  i  izemren  ad  aɣ-yinin  acu  yeḍran  s  tidet. 

 
 
- 13 - 

 

Nessawel-as i ukumisar, ur yettɛeṭṭil ara ad yili gar-aneɣ, 
d netta ara aɣ-d-yinin d acu ilaq ad nexdem. 
  Wehmeɣ,  qqureɣ,  ur  ufiɣ  d  acu  ad  d-iniɣ.  Tinɣiman ? 
Anwa  ara  yamnen  d  akken  mmi-s  n  Si Racid  ad  ineɣ 
iman-is ?  Ayɣer  ara  ineɣ  Nabil  iman-is ?  D  anelmad 
asdawan, seg twacult turdkidt, iḥemmel tudert dayen kan, 
ayɣer  ad  yerr  ihi  talast  i  tudert-is,  yernu  sdat  n  uxxam  n 
yimawlan-is ? 
 
Ɣlint-d  fell-i  tikta  am  uḥemmal  n  waman.  Cwi  kan 
suffɣent-iyi tyitwin n tewwura n ṭumubilat d leswat n kra 
n  yimdanen  seg  uɣraq  ideg  lliɣ.  Iruḥ-d  ukumisar  ɣer 
tama-nneɣ  s  tazzla,  zzin-as-d  sin  n  yimsulta,  yiwen  deg-
sen  s  yiselsa  iɣarimen,  yeṭṭef  ddaw  n  teɣraḍt-is  yiwen  n 
uqrab.Yejbed  umsaltu  aɛessas  iman-is  akken  ad  yeǧǧ 
abrid i wid i d-yusan. Qqimen ttezzin ɣef tfekka, ttakken-
d  yiwet  n  tugna  am  wakken  seg  wid  yessnen  uffiren  n 
tmenɣiwin. Yekna bab n uqrab ɣef tfekka yeẓẓlen, yessers 
tagecrirt-is tayeffust ɣef tmurt, yeqɛed nnwaḍer-is, ikerrec 
icenfiren-is,  ihuzz  aqerruy-is,  iban  yewhem  deg  wayen 
yettwali ;  yessers  sakin  afus-is  ddaw  n  uqerru  n  lmegget 
akken ad yerfed s laɛqel tafekka-nni iwakken ad yessuffeɣ 
afus-nni  yeṭṭfen 
sakin  aqrab-is, 
tameẓyant.  Yeldi 
yessuffeɣ-d tayuga n tqeffazin d yiwet n teckart tamecṭuḥt 
tafrawant.  Yeṭṭef  tameẓyant,  idewwer-itt  s  laɛqel  kan, 
yerra-tt daxel n teckart. Yebda sakin aqelleb deg ljerḥ-nni s 
yiḍuḍan-is.  Uẓaɣ  ɣer  ukumisar  n  temsulta,  iban  ur  iyi-
iwali ara. 

 
 
- 14 - 

 

Ihuzz aqerruy-is, yeqqim yettxemmim, sakin yenṭeq : 

Amek  i  tettiliḍ  a  Si  Aḥmed ?  D  acu-tent  tikta-inek 
timenza ? 
  Yezzi-d ɣur-i, yewhem : 
Ah  d  kečč  a  « ustad »…  ur  iyi-d-tenniḍ  ara  deg  uɣerbaz-
agi alemmas i tzedɣeḍ. 
—Ala,  dagi  i  xedmeɣ  zik  uqbel  ad  uɣaleɣ  d  amastan. 
Yernu  Racid  Benɣusa,  anemhal  aqdim,  d  yiwen  seg 
yimeddukkal-iw  imeqqranen.  D  mmi-s  i  tettwaliḍ  yeẓẓel 
sdat-k… 
 
Anda i yella baba-s ? Neḥwaǧ ad nesɛu kra n  yisallen. 
  Racid Benɣusa ur iḥerrek ara seg umkan-is. Yerfed kan 
aqerruy-is,  yembawel  ciṭuḥ  kan.  Imuqel  ɣer  wid  yellan 
sdat-s,  yenṭeq-d  s  laɛqel,  ad  as-tiniḍ  i  yiman-is  kan  i 
ihedder. 
  Ur  ẓriɣ  ara…  ur  ẓriɣ  ara  acu  yeḍran.  Mi  d-uɣaleɣ  s 
axxam  ɣef  lɛecra  n  yiḍ,  ufiɣ  Nabil…  yessusem,  am 
wakken yebɣa ad yernu tanfalit niḍen, ahat awal « mmi », 
ahat ad fell-as  yeɛfu  yerḥem, maca yessed ɣef tuɣmas-is, 
ikemmel  sakin  ameslay.  Ufiɣ-t  yeqqim  deg  usalun,  ɣef 
tgecrar-is  yiwet  n  tezmamt,  deg  ufus-is  amru.  Mi  i  yi-
iwala  kan,  yeɣleq  tazmamt-is  s  temɣawla.  Ur  d-yerri  ara 
fell-i  ssalam.  Yezzi-d  ɣur-i,  imuqel-iyi-d  s  temɣawla, 
idewwer aqerruy-is fell-i am wakken tella yiwet n tɣawsa 
i  yebɣa  ad  yeffer  fell-i.  Ḥulfaɣ  am  wakken  tella  yiwet  n 
lḥaǧa  n  dir  i  yeffer  fell-i.  Ɛlakuliḥal,  mačči  d  tikkelt 
tamezwarut  ideg  nettnaɣ,  ladɣa  seg  wasmi  iserreḥ  i 
učamar,  yelsa  tacacit,  yerna  aqendur.  Maca  nnuba-a  ur

yenṭiq ula s yiwen n wawal. Yekker, iruḥ srid ɣer texxamt-

yeqqar  s  utram,  am  leɛwayed-is,  tisurtin  n  Leqran. 
Kecmeɣ  ɣer  texxamt-iw,  ssut-is  mazal  yettaweḍ  ɣer 
yimezzaɣ-iw.  Temeṭṭut-iw  tella  teṭṭes.  Sliɣ  sakin  i  ssut  n 
tewwurt,  faqeɣ  yeffeɣ.  Bɣiɣ  ad  kkreɣ  ɣur-s  akken  ad  t-
qenɛeɣ    ur  itteffeɣ  ara  deg  tlemmast  n  yiḍ,  maca  ur 
xdimeɣ  acemma,  qqimeɣ  kan  deg  umkan-iw.  Zrin  tura 
qrib  sin  n  yiseggasen  seg  wasmi  yuɣal  uqrur-nni  amḍuɛ 
ur  iyi-yettaɣ  ara  awal.  Yuɣal  d  aballaɣ,  d  axfafan,  ur 
iqebbel ara irkelli acu i as-qqareɣ. Yiwen n ubrid nennuɣ. 
Ɛerḍeɣ  ad  as-sfehmeɣ  belli  tarbaɛt-agi  i  yeṭṭafar  ur  tebɣi 
lxir  la  i  tmurt  wala  i  yimezdaɣ-is.  D  tarbaɛt  i  yeffɣen  i 
ubrid,  tetteffer  deffir  n  usɣan  d ddin  akken  ad  tḥudd  ɣef 
tenfatin  n  Marikan  tamnukdit  d  tgeldiwin  tiɛrabin. 
Tirbuyaɛ  n  lǧihad  n  Afɣanistan,  d  Marikan  tamnukdit 
yellan  deffir-nsent  akken  ad  tewwet  yis-sent  Russya

tenfatin 
leslaḥ.   Amennuɣ,  d  amennuɣ  ɣef 
refden 
tidemsanin,  mačči  d  amennuɣ  ɣef  usɣan  neɣ  ɣef  teflest.

wudem-is.  Muqleɣ-t  kan,  ulac  acu  i  as-nniɣ.  Uyseɣ  seg

Lmuhim… tagi d tudert-iw, nekk d amasay fell-as. Ass-agi

ugar n mraw n yisebtar, armi i yi-yessexleɛ ssut n tersast.

nsel i ssut niḍen ara yerẓen tasusmi n yiḍ. Nerǧa s tsusmi.

n tsusmi taẓayant. Ulac win i izemren ad as-yegzem awal. 
S lḥir ameqqran i nerǧa ad ikemmel awal.

refden  idlisen  iẓayanen  n  usɣan,  belli  ula  d  tameṭṭut-is 
yeṭṭef-itt  waṭṭan  n  « tmesɣanit »  i  d-yeglan  s  uzegzaw  d 
uquran. Tuɣal ur teṭṭixir ara i yimaṭṭafen n usɣan n tmurt 
n Ssaɛudiya d Maser, tettẓalla deg lawan, yernu tettẓumm 
ussan  n  warim  d  umhad.  Ahat  d  aṭṭan  n  ukunsir  i  tt-
yeṭṭfen  deg  wagguren-a 
i  yellan  deffir  n 
ubeddel-a, ɣas ma imejjayen d tesleḍt qqaren-d belli aṭṭan-
is yerked, yernu yella usirem akken ad teḥlu. Mi d-nuɣal, 
yernu mačči d leɛwayed-is, ur yeḥbis ara ameslay ɣef tikli 
tamaynut  n  tmeṭṭut-is.  Askasi  akked  tmeṭṭut-is  yuɣal  ur 
yettɛeddi ara awal ɣef lumur n uxxam. 
  Tameṭṭut  n  umeddakkel-iw  yesseɛya-tt  mliḥ  waṭṭan. 
Aṭas  i  as-iruḥen  seg  thuski-ines.  Udem-is  yuɣal  d  awraɣ, 
allen-is  iruḥ-asent  ucraraq-nsent.  Akka  i  tga  ddunit,  ulac 
lḥaǧa ara yeqqimen am wakken tella deg tazwara, d wagi 
d  alugan  amezwaru  d  uneggaru  iɣef  ibedd  ugama. 
Neqqim  kra  n  lweqt  nettales  kan  i  tenfaliyin  n  uɛezzi  i 
neqqar deg tegnatin  am  ta,  numen neɣ  ur numin ara yis-
sent, armi nesla i ladan i aɣ-igezmen awal, yerreẓ tasusmi 
n tefrara i yebdan afriri. Beddeɣ s tmara, ɛyiɣ mačči d kra, 
sellmeɣ fell-asen, snesreɣ iman-iw deg tsusmi.

staɛerfen.  Ffɣen  i  ubrid,  d  imnafqen,  kerhen  adabu  d 

 
 
- 31 - 

 

yinawen-ines  i  ten-yesguǧǧen  seg  tudrin-nsen  i  d-yezgan

Ula  leswaq  n  ufellaḥ,  tiḥunna-nni  timeqqranin  yesnuzun

d  yisufar  niḍen  n  lebni.  Akka,  deg  mraw  n  yiseggasen 
kan,  rewlen  medden  seg  yigran  d  lluzinat,  uɣalen  d 
imsenza, kecmen amaḍal n lbiɛ d ccra. Ṭṭef, awi-d ɣer da, 
« cedd,  medd »  am  wakken  i  d-qqaren.  Ulac  laɛqed,  ulac

ad  tt-senzen  i  yimsenza.  Tuɣal-d  lqella  n  sselɛa  tettbin-d

ssuffɣen i lbiɛ. Ifri n Ɛali-baba, maca mebla iɛessasen. Ala 
xaṭi,  d  iɛessasen-ines  i  yuɣalen  d  imakaren,  d  nitni  i  tt-
yukren.  Akka

ara  ula  yiwet  n  ddqiqa  deg  yimeslayen-is  belli  ayen  i 
ixeddem irkelli yeffeɣ i ubrid n usaḍuf. 
  D  tagi  i  d  Ɛayn-el-kerma  n  wass-a…  tceqqeq,  tewwet

amẓur, tessekcam deg wul leḥzen d tuggdi. Asirem-inek : 
tarewla seg umkan-agi deg lkar tamezwarut.

tabeḥbaḥt  n  Caɛban  i  aɣ-d-yeqqaren    d  tigi  i  d  tiqbucin

ayɣer ur tettekseḍ ara ihi irkassen-ik n umsedrar akken ad 
teknuḍ  ɣef  tẓerbit  yeččuren  s  tɣebbart.  Dɣa  ad  ikerrec 
Caɛban  icenfiren-is  izuranen  wa  ad  yini :  nekk  d  amaziɣ,

« imi  d  amucar  i  yi-tettwalim,  ihi  ɛuhdeɣ  Rebbi  ur  tt-id-
uɣaleɣ ɣer yifri-agi n yiɣerdayen. Ad ɛeddiɣ tura srid ɣer

lǧameɛ  ad  ẓalleɣ  ad  ken-senzeɣ  i  yimehbal  n  Yakuc.  Ad

as-yerr  Caɛban :  « Iban  ṛeggmen-ak  amkan  yelhan  deg

Ssneɣ  aṭas  seg  yimidawen-ik  ifesyanen  i  ibeddlen  iselsa-
nsen n yiserdasen s uqendur d tcacit, zwaren, ṭṭfen lesfuf 
imezwura  n  yimeẓulla,  yewwi-ten  ṭṭmeɛ ».  Mi  ara  tekres 
taluft,  nessekcem  iman-nneɣ.  Ad  nbedd  irkelli,  ad  neṭṭef 
Ɛebdella  seg  yiɣallen,  ad  t-nḥellel  akken  ad  yuɣal  ad 
yeqqim  wa  ad  nkemmel  aqesser.  Caɛban,  yettuɣal  ɣer 
lecɣal-is,  iseffeḍ  lkisan,  yesɛedday  acifun  ɣef  ukunṭwar. 
Ad  d-tuɣal  talwit  ɣer  ṭṭabla-nneɣ.  Ad  yebdu  Racid 
ameslay,  awal-is  yebɛed  ɣef  usentel  n  umennuɣ.  Ad 
nkemmel  awal  armi  kkawen  yimawen-nneɣ.  Askasi  ad 
yuɣal d lehdur war anamek, ladɣa ma ḥman yiqerra-nneɣ.

nnfaq  d  tekriḍt.  Nekk  d  aselmad  n  umezruy,  ssneɣ 
amezruy  n  tmurt-a,  awines  awines,  tardast  tardast.  Ulac

yettnaɣen ɣef yignan i tkessawt d wakal yelhan i tfellaḥt.

ɣer  wakal-nneɣ,  yezmer  lḥal  ad  dduklen  leɛrac-agi  kra  n

fell-i s yisem-iw. Iban yessen-iyi, maca ur t-ɛqileɣ ara bib-
bih.  Sakin  yesseqsa-yi-d  ma  yella  ccreɛ  ass-a.  Ur  ufiɣ  ara

Idmaren n umɣar tuɣ-iten ttuzagen seg wurfan, yufa-tt d 
tagnit  akken  ad  yeṭṭerḍeq :  « Ilef-nni  i  yebran  i  yelli  s 
kraḍet  n  temcicin,  tameqqrant  deg-sent  ur  tessaweḍ  ara 
ukkuẓ  n  yiseggasen,  yernu  tḥeḍreḍ  a  « ustad »,  ssarameɣ 
ur tettuḍ ara ɣas akken ɛeddan tura kra n yiseggasen fell-
as,  yugi  umelɛun-nni  ad  d-yefk  nnafaqa  i  yefreḍ  fell-as 
unezzarfu.  Heḍreɣ-as  acḥal  d  abrid  s  laɛqel,  maca  argaz-
nni  am  tata,  yezga  yettbeddil  rray-is.  Iṛeggem,  maca  ur 
yettaṭṭaf  ara  deg  wawal-is.  Nessufeɣ-as-d  lkarṭa.  Deg 
tazwara yeḥseb iman-is ur zriɣ acu, ur yettak ccan i yiwen. 
Yenna-as unezzarfu ad t-yessekcem ɣer lḥebs ma ur ixelles 
ara  nnafaqa.  Seg  uyaẓiḍ  yuɣal  d 
tayaẓiḍt.  Yebda 
imeṭṭawen,  yeccetka  i  unezzarfu  ɣef  yir  tagnit  ideg 
yettidir.  Yenna-as-d    ur  ixeddem  ara.  Nekk  ssneɣ-t  mliḥ, 
yezdeɣ  yid-neɣ  deg  « lebrarik ».  Ixeddem  d  abennay  ɣer 
medden.  Ttwaliɣ-t  yal  tameddit  mi  ara  d-yuɣal  yumes  s 
ssiman  d  ssbiɣa.  Ass-nni  yeggul  ad  yeffeɣ  kan  sɣur 
unezzarfu ad ixelles ddin-is. Aggur umbaɛd iḍegger-aɣ-d 
ufuḥan  agim  n  yidinaren.  Acu  ara  nexdem  s  wagim  n 
yidinaren ?  Ur  keffunt  ara  ula  i  uyefki  n  llufanat.  Yuɣal 
irewwel  fell-i.  Ttnadiɣ  fell-as  deg  uxxam-is,  ur  d-itteffeɣ 
ara ɣur-i. Mi ara iyi-iwali seg mbaɛɛid, ad ibeddel abrid-is.

Ilef mmi-s n yilef, iɣil ddunit-a ur tesɛi ara leqwanen. Ad

yessekcem ɣer lḥebs. Bɣiɣ ad t-waliɣ daxel n bu-yikurdan 
mebla tafat i kra n wagguren, ad ixelles tucmit i yexdem. 
Ur nebɣi ara idrimen-is, nuɣ tannumi i lḥif d laẓ. D Rebbi 
subḥanu  i irezzqen… ». 
  Mi  yella  umɣar  yessuffuɣ  ayen  yellan  deg  wul-iw, 
mektaɣ-d  tessuter  deg-i  taɣdemt  ad    ḥuddeɣ  ɣef  yelli-s 
semmus  n  yiseggasen  aya.  S  laɛqel  kan  tuɣal-d  tawlift  n 
yiwet  n  tlemẓit  ur  nessaweḍ  ara  snat  n  tmerwin  n 
yiseggasen,  tettel  deg  yiwen  n  lḥijab  d  aqehwi,  teṭṭef  gar 
yifassen-is  yiwen  n  llufan,  snat  n  teqcicin  timeẓyanin 
yeffeɣ-itent laɛqel, uggadent, ṭṭfen-tt seg yiḍarren. Tenna : 
« Ireggem-iyi,  yekkat-iyi  mebla  ssebba.  Yettɛayar-iyi  s 
yemma-s n tullas. Sebreɣ, nniɣ-as ahat ad aɣ-yerzeq Rebbi 
s  uqcic.  Maca  seg  wasmi  d-tlul  teqcict  tis  kraḍet,  ihaj, 
yejhel.  Yuɣal  ihedder  yid-i  s  rregmet,  yekkat-iyi  kan. 
Yuɣal  yettara  zzɛaf-is  deg  tullas,  ireggem-itent,  yekkat-
itent  s  rrkel  ɣef  wulac ».  Yezzem-it  mliḥ  unezzarfu, maca

watmaten-is.  Maca  yesseḥbes-it  unezzarfu, 
iwexxer

dduxan.  Mazal  ur  tt-suffɣeɣ  ara  seg  lǧib-iw    armi  walaɣ

tesselmed  ddunit.  Akken  ad  tizmireḍ  ad  tɛeddiḍ  i

waya, ilaq ad tefkeḍ azal i yiselsa-inek, akustim azedgan d 
tekrabaḍt  tahuskayt,  akken  ad  tbineḍ  mačči  d  menwala, 
wa ad ak-qadren yimdanen, ur k-ḥeqqren ara. Nekk uɣeɣ 
tannumi  yal  mi  ara  seɛɛuɣ  ccɣel  deg  tedbelt,  neɣ  yal  mi 
ara ruḥeɣ ad waliɣ yiwen seg yimasayen, ɣas d ameẓyan, 
ttlusuɣ  akustim  d  tekrabaḍt,  seffḍeɣ  mliḥ  issebbaḍen-iw 
iberkanen.    Yernu  seg  wasmi  kecmeɣ  tasdawit,  yuɣal 
ukustim  ur  i  yi-yeṭṭixir  ara  am  uqrab.  Imi  ɣelbeɣ 

 
 
- 57 - 

 

inelmaden  niḍen  deg 
laɛmer,  uɣalen  ssawalen-iyi 
« Ustad ». Aẓayer-agi yesnerna deg temɣer-inu, yeččur ul-
iw s tumert. 
  Walaɣ  deg  wudem  n  tneflust,  ɛerqent-as  ciṭuḥ,    tebɣa 
ad  iyi-tesseqsi  ɣef  ssebba  iyi-d-yewwin,  maca  ulac  acu 
texdem.  Tessuter  deg-i  ad  qqimeɣ,  tekcem  ɣer  Si  Nasser. 
Ula  nekk  ɛerqent-iyi,  ur  ẓriɣ  ara  amek  ara  s-mmeslayeɣ 
ɣef wugur-inu, semraseɣ kra n tefyar d tenfaliyin, tikwal s 
taɛrabt taɣurbizt, tikwal s tantala n taɛrabt, maca amastan 
yessafeg  kulci  mi  iyi-d-yerra  s  tefransit  –  yernu  ilaq  ad 
teẓreḍ  d  acu-tt  tafransisst-nni ?  –  uqbel  ma  ad  yessuter 
deg-i ad d-aɣeɣ amkan. Imir-n kan fehmeɣ la ttmeslayeɣ d 
umastan  afransawal.  Yernu  mi  meyyzeɣ  acḥal  n 
yiseggasen  fell-as,  fkiɣ-as  ass-nni  semmuset  n  tmerwin  n 
yiseggasen,  ad  yili  gar  yimestanen  imezwura,  seg  wid 
yeɣran  deg  Fransa.  Amek  ad  mmeslayeɣ  yid-s,  nekk  ur 
nessin mliḥ tutlayt n « Voltaire », am wakken i as-semman 
At n taɛrabt d useɛreb deg tesdawit. D tidet, qqareɣ yis-s 
aɣmis,  maca  asusru-inu  yeɛwej,  yeseḍsay.  Ayɣer,  mačči 
seg zzawiya n Sidi Ɛbid i d-fruriɣ ? Lemdeɣ qrib mraw n 
yixfawen  n  Luqran.  Tewweḍ-d  timmunent,  neffeɣ  seg 
umadaɣ-nneɣ  nruḥ  ɣer    taddart  n  Sidi  Ɛmer.  Maca  mi 
ɛeddaɣ  mraw  d  sin  n  yiseggasen,  yewɛer-iyi  lḥal  ad 
kecmeɣ  ɣer  uɣerbaz  am  warrac  niḍen.  Sdukklen-aɣ, 
nekkni i aɣ-teǧǧa tmacint n uselmed, deg yiwet n tneɣrit, 
wwin-aɣ-d yiwet  n  tefransit ara  aɣ-yeslemden  agemmay 
n tutlayt. Tecbeḥ mačči d kra, tesderwec-aɣ, tesker-d yakk 
lemcihwat  yeṭṭsen  deg-neɣ.  Tuɣ-aɣ  meqqrit,  nettnaɣ

ttruḥuɣ  ad  xedmeɣ  deg  lfirmat  i  aɣ-d-yezzin  akken  ad 
negmer llubyan d ṭumaṭic. Terra-iyi yemma ɣer zzawiya n 
Ccix  Lmulud,  maca  ufiɣ  iman-iw  d  acaraf  gar  warrac  d 
imeẓyanen,  yernu  tarrayt-nni  n  wallus  mebla  tigzi 
tesserfa-yi mliḥ, dɣa ad ffɣeɣ gar yisuɣan-nni, ur ttuɣaleɣ 
ara. Acḥal n tikkal i d-icetka Ccix seg yibaten-inu. Yiwet n 
tmeddit, yekcem-d gma yefreḥ, yenna-yi-d ilaq ad heggiɣ 
iman-iw  i  tuɣalin  ɣer  leqraya.  Ur  as-fkiɣ  ara  azal  i  usali, 
ɣur-i nekkini, tikti n tuɣalin ɣer uɣerbaz teffeɣ i lebda seg 
wallaɣ-iw.  D  acu  ara  xedmeɣ  deg  tlemmast  n  warrac 
imeẓyanen ? Amer d lebɣi, ad iyi-yessidef d axeddam deg 
lfirma.  Imuqel-iyi-d  s  yiwet  n  tmuɣli  i  yeskecmen  tuggdi 
deg  wul-iw.  Yella,  fell-as  ad  yaɛfu,  yerḥem,  yewɛer,  ur 
yessugut  ara  awal.  Yezga  yectekay  seg  uxeddim  deg 
lfirma, yeqqar-aɣ-d ilaq kan i yimɣaren d temɣarin, mačči 
i  yilmeẓyen.  Yekcem  d  ameẓyan  ɣer  lɛesker,  ur  neẓri  ara 
amek  i  yemmut  umeɣbun.  D  netta  i  yellan  d  asalel  n 
uxxam,  yemma  tettaɣ-as  awal,  txeddem  yakk  ayen  i  as-
yeqqar.  Yemma  tedda  yid-s.  Leqraya  d  tasarut,  d  abrid 
uɣdim,  yernu  keččini  tlemdeḍ  Luqran,  teɣriḍ  sin  n 
yiseggasen  deg  uɣerbaz,  yaɛni  ulac  acu  i  tlemdeḍ ?  Gma 
tuɣ-it  ussan-nni  deg  lɛesker.  Yelsa  iselsa-nni  n  userdas, 
yewwi-yi  ɣer  uɣerbaz,  yessekles-iyi  deg  temsirin  n 
tmeddit  yettwaxedmen  i  yimeqqran  i  teǧǧa  leqraya  am 
tmital-iw. Yemma tezga tessebɣas deg-i akken ad ẓewreɣ 
deg  leqraya,  ahat  ad  afeɣ  axeddim  yelhan  ara  yeglun  s 
tjernaḍt tameqqrant. Akka i ssawḍeɣ ad kemmleɣ leqraya-
inu. Urɛad ssawḍeɣ snat n tmerwin n yiseggasen, wwḍeɣ 

 
 
- 60 - 

 

ɣer  yiwen  n  uswir  i  yi-yeǧǧan  ad  kecmeɣ  ɣer  uɣerbaz  n 
usileɣ n yiselmaden. Maca rniɣ ressiɣ timusniwin-inu deg 
tutlayt  tafransisst  deg  yiseggasen-nni  asmi  lliɣ  ttheggiɣ 
akayad  n  lbak.  Maca  ɣas  akken,  ẓriɣ  xusseɣ  mliḥ  deg 
tutlayt-agi. 
 
Si  Nasser,  meqqer  ciṭuḥ  deg  laɛmer,  d  arqaqan,  yelsa 
aselsu  awinaɣ  mebla  takrabaḍt,  cclaɣem-is  d  irqaqanen, 
udem-is mellul. Nniɣ-d d yiman-iw : wagi ama d aqbayli 
neɣ  d  ajijli.  Iḥesses-iyi  mliḥ  mi  as-ḥkiɣ  ugur-inu.  Ihuzz 
aqerruy-is, yenna : 
—Keččini seg wigi i yeɣran s taɛrabt, ur ɣliḍeɣ ara ? 
  Yesduqes-iyi useqsi-ines, dɣa rriɣ-as s temɣawla : 
—Ih, maca ssneɣ ciṭuḥ tafransisst. Ur ttmeslayeɣ ara yis-s 
s sshala, maca qqareɣ yis-s war uguren ? 
  Yezmumeg, yenna s yiwet n taɣect yeččuren s leḥzen : 
—Aseɛreb  yettaɣ  yal  amkan.  Qqaren-d  agezdu  n 
tmussniwin tizerfanin ad  yuɣal yesɣray  s taɛrabt kan seg 
unekcum asdawan i d-iteddun. 
—Akka  i  d-qqaren.  Ssneɣ  kra  n  yinelmaden  n  tneɣriyin 
yeqqaren  s  tefransist,  ḥeddren  yid-neɣ  deg  temsirin  s 
taɛrabt. Kra deg-sen uɣalen ɣer tneɣrit yeqqaren s taɛrabt. 
 
Ikerrec Si Nasser icenfiren-is, ihuzz aqerruy-is, yenna : 
—Tamacint  n  useɛreb  tettazzal.  Yessefk  fell-aɣ  ad  naɣ 
amkan  deg-s  ma  ulac  ad  aɣ-yeǧǧ  lweqt.  Uggadeɣ  ad  aɣ-
teḍru  am  wat  iḍarren  iberkanen,  ad  d-naf  iman-nneɣ 
nettuḥetem ad neǧǧ tamurt. 
  Yessusem ciṭuḥ, tamuɣli-ines tezger idurar, ad as-tiniḍ 
yemmekta-d  kra  n  ccfawat  n  leḥzen.  Lliɣ  ttmeslayeɣ  s 

 
 
- 61 - 

 

tentala n taɛrabt, sya ɣer da ad skecmeɣ kra n yimeslayen 
s tefransist akken ad t-qenɛeɣ belli ssawaleɣ akken iwata s 
tutlayt  n  « Voltaire ».  Netta,  yella  yettmeslay  s  tefransist, 
yessexdam seg lweqt ɣer wayeḍ awalen n tantala taɛrabt. 
Asusru-ines  i  wawalen  s  taɛrabt  yettemcabi  ɣer  ususru-
inu  i  wawalen  s  tefransist,  d  askerker.  Ihuzz  aqerruy-is, 
yenna : 
—Aneɣlaf-agi  amaynut  n  teɣdemt  yettbin-d  yekreh 
tafransisst,  yettheggi  iman-is  ad  yesseɛreb  tadbelt  n 
teɣdemt irkelli. Iḍelli kan yella ɣur-i yiwen n umezlu deg 
uxxam  n  teɣdemt  n  Lḥerrac,  yesseḥbes-iyi  unezzarfu,  d 
ilemẓi  ur  nessaweḍ  ara  kraḍet  n  tmerwin  n  yiseggasen 
deg  laɛmer-is,  mi  lliɣ  ttmeslayeɣ  s  tefransist,  twalaḍ  s 
anda nessaweḍ ? Nniɣ-as : « Ulac asaḍuf i igedlen asemres 
n  tefransist ».  Yenna-d  d  tanaḍin  n  uneɣlaf  amaynut, 
tḥettem  ɣef  yimestanen  ad  smersen  tutlayt  taɣelnawt. 
Nniɣ :  « Ayɣer  i  as-tessemmaḍ  tutlayt  taɣelnawt,  ayɣer 
mačči tutlayt taɛrabt ? ». Yenna-d s zzux d nnefxa ur nesɛi 
lmaɛna :  « Sel  a  « ustad »  …  nekkni  d  inezzurfa  ur 
nxeddem  ara  tasertit,  nekkni  nessanas  isuḍaf  n  Uwanak 
azzayri  u  Awanak  azzayri  amunan  yeqqar-d  yessefk  ɣef 
yimestanen  ad  smersen  tutlayt  taɣelnawt  yellan  d  tutlayt 
taɛrabt.  Uma  tafransisst  d  tutlayt  taberranit,  d  tutlayt  n 
umnekcam,  yernu  waqila  amnekcam  yeffeɣ  yakan  seg 
tmurt-nneɣ ».  Nniɣ :  « Tamharsa  tafransisst  nḥareb-itt  s 
tutlayt-is.  Ur  ẓriɣ  ara  ma  teẓriḍ  belli  alɣu  n  umenzu  n 
wunbir  yura  deg  tazwara  s  trumit,  suqlen-t-id  s  taɛrabt 
umbaɛd,  yernu  tuget  n  yimḍebbren  d  yimeqqran  n 

 
 
- 62 - 

 

tegrawla  llan  d  ifransawalen ».  Yegzem-iyi  awal,  yenna : 
« Ur bɣiɣ ara ad kecmeɣ yid-k deg uskasi aserti. Mmeslay 
s taɛrabt neɣ susem. Asaḍuf d asaḍuf ». Xemmemeɣ ciṭuḥ 
dɣa  nniɣ-as :  « Ad  d-meslayeɣ  ihi  s  tentala  taɛrabt.  Ur 
cukkeɣ ara tettwaḥseb d tutlayt taberranit ? ». Ɣileɣ dayen 
nufa  tifrat  i  wugur,  maca  mi  s-fkiɣ  asarag  n  ustan  akken 
ad  t-yessidef  deg  ukaram,  yenna :  « Isaragen  n  ustan 
yuran  ad  ilin  daɣen  s  tutlayt  taɣelnawt ».  Kkreɣ  akked 
yimestanen niḍen yellan din. Maca anezzarfu-nni ur yecliɛ 
ara  deg-neɣ.  Neccetka  ɣer  win  iwumi  ssemman  medden 
« aɣerraq ».  Yenna :  « Fehmeɣ  ugur-nwen,  maca  ulac  acu 
zemreɣ  ad  awen-xedmeɣ.  Tanaḍin  d  tanaḍin.  Yernu  ad 
awen-xebbreɣ  d  akken  anezzarfu-agi  amaynut  yesɛa 
yiwen  deg  lɛesker  i  ibedden  ɣer  yidi-s,  yettḥuddu-t. 
Teẓram axir-iw amek i tleḥḥu tmurt-nneɣ. Ur tturareɣ ara 
s uɣrum n warraw-iw. Ma tuɣem awal-iw, lemdet taɛrabt 
neɣ  awit-d  albaɛḍ  ad  ken-iɛiwnen  deg  useɛreb  n 
warraten-nwen ».  Mi  d-neffeɣ,  yenna-yi-d  yiwen  seg 
yimestanen  i  yesnecnicen  belli  laɛǧeb-agi  yesselḥay-it 
yiwen n ukulunil, kra qqaren d gma-s n tmeṭṭut tis snat n 
yiwen  n    ukulunil,  tin  i  iteddun  yid-s  deg  yinigen 
ibaxusiyen ɣer tmunaɣ n Yuruba. Am wakken i tettwaliḍ, 
nekk ɣriɣ deg tallit n Fransa, deg lawan-nni neqqar taɛrabt 
yiwet n temsirt deg waggur, ulac win i as-yefkan azal. Ula 
d  tantala  taɛrabt  ur  tt-ssineɣ  ara.  Nekk  d  aqbayli,  seg 
temdint  n  Ɛin-el-ḥemmam.  Tameṭṭut-iw  kif-kif.  Deg 
uxxam  nettmeslay  s  teqbaylit  kan.  Aql-iyi  s  tidet  deg 
lmerta.  Ad  beddleɣ  tawuri-inu  ɣer  taggara  n  ddunit-iw ? 

 
 
- 63 - 

 

Suɣeɣ s lferḥ d tumert : 

Ad  ddmeɣ  leḥwali-w    ad  laḥqeɣ  At-yiḍarren  iberkanen ? 
Nitni  d  ifransiyen,  uɣalen  ɣer  tmurt  n  lejdud-nsen.  Maca 
nekkni  sani  ad  nruḥ ?  Ɣer  tmurt  n  Leqbayel ?  Aseɛreb ad 
tt-yaweḍ  yiwen  n  wass.  Tutlayt  taqbaylit  d  tantala 
taɣerfant, ur tettwaru, ur tettwaɣer, yernu ur staɛerfen ara 
yis-s s talɣa tunsibt. 
  Yessusem ciṭuḥ, yerna-d deg wawal-is : 
—Maca  yewwi-k-id  Rebbi  deg  lawan.  (Yenna-tt-id  s 
tantala taɛrabt, ula nekk ulseɣ-as deg wul-iw : yewwi-yi-d 
Rebbi,  d  tidet…)  Kečč  tettnadiḍ  ɣef  tannant  ara  k-yeldin 
tiwwura  n  twuri  n  umastan,  nekk  ḥwaǧeɣ  win  ara  iyi-
iɛiwnen deg tsuqilt n warraten, yernu ttxemmimeɣ s tidet 
ad lemdeɣ taɛrabt. 
 
—Qebleɣ  asumer-inek.  Ula  d  nekk  d  tagnit  ideg  ara 
lemdeɣ deg-s tafransisst. 
—Nemtafaq a « ustad ». 
  Ttaḍsaɣ seg wawal n « ustad », nniɣ : 
—D keččini d « ustad » a « Maître ». 
  Yezmumeg,  yenna :  « ‘Maître’,  ‘Ustad’,  …  ack-iten 
wawalen-agi, maca ini-yi-d anwa i ten-yuklalen s tidet ? 
 
Ibedd,  isellem  fell-i,  dɣa  walaɣ  udem-is  amek  i 
yennecraḥ.  Imir-n  faqeɣ  belli  d  alemmas  deg  lqedd,    d 
ṭṭɛafa n tfekka-ines kan i t-id-yeskanyen d awezzlan. 
  Akka  i  kecmeɣ  ɣer  twuri  n  umastan  seg  tawwurt-ines 
tahrawant.  Timlilit  akked  Si  Nasser,  tura  ad  tt-id-iniɣ  s 
zzux, i iɛeddan fell-as ugar n snat n tmerwin n yiseggasen, 
tbeddel tikli n tudert-iw. Yid-s i lemdeɣ tawuri n umastan 

 
 
- 64 - 

 

d  wuffiren-ines,  lhan  neɣ  dir-iten.  Lemdeɣ  belli  asaḍuf  d 
arekti  tzemreḍ  ad  t-tɛerkeḍ  amek  i  k-yehwa.  Yuɣal  Si 
Nasser  d  ameddakkel,  d  amidaw,  nettemɛawen  ar  iḍ-a 
deg  waṭas  n  yiwezla.  Tennerna  tdukli-nneɣ  mliḥ  asmi 
neṭṭef rray ad nesbedd yiwet n tesqamut ara iḥudden ɣef 
yimeḥbas  isertiyen  d  yineɣmasen.  Yeqqim  ibeddi-nneɣ 
ɣer  yidi-s  n  yimeḥbas  n  umussu  amaziɣ  d  lecyux  n 
umussu  ineslem  d  amselɣu  s  wayes  nettzuxxu,  acku 
yerra-d i twuri n umastan lqima d wazal-is umbaɛd mi tt-
ssamsen wid yettazzalen deffir n yidrimen d udabu. 
  Ulac  acu  ara  ffreɣ  fell-awen  ma  nniɣ-awen-d  lliɣ 
ttwaliɣ deg tawuri n umastan s yiwet nniya d tameqqrant. 
Ayen  i  yi-ijebden  deg  tazwara  ɣer  twuri-agi,  d  idrimen. 
Yernu yessefk fell-i ad staɛerfeɣ belli kniɣ ddaw n uɣway 
n  yidrimen  d  tlawin.  Sin-agi  ur  zmireɣ  ara  ad  d-beddeɣ 
mgal-nsen. Acḥal i swiɣ seg snat n tliwa-agi yesderwicen. 
Acḥal  d  abrid  i  skerkreɣ  nnif-iw  deg  waluḍ-nsen.  Maca 
ɣas  akken  iqurar-ines  fessusit  ɣef  tid  i  t-ittekken  seg 
udabu.  Urǧin  yesseḍmeɛ-iyi  udabu,  am  wakken  i  teḍra  i 
waṭas  seg  yimidawen-inu  i  irekḍen  imenzayen-nsen, 
ḍelmen  imdanen  ulac  acu  xedmen,  skecmen-ten  ɣer 
leḥbus,  acku  iruḥ-asen-d  lamer  seg  uwsawen,  dɣa  uɣen 
imekwan,  kra  deg-sen  uɣalen  d  ineɣlafen.  Akkagi  i 
lemdeɣ seg Si Nasser. 
  Maca ɣas akken, amastan ɣur-i d win  yettḥuddun ɣef 
wid  yettuḍelmen,  ɣef  teɣtas.  Ẓriɣ  yakan  kra  n  yisura 
skanayen-d amek i ixeddem umastan akken ad isellek wid 
yettuḍelmen  seg  terdayin  ur  nesɛi  lsas  wa  ad  yessemneɛ

imi  seg-sen 

  yiwen  n  uneḍlib  i 

iqerra-nsen  seg  lfinga.  Zgiɣ  ttbeddayeɣ  ɣer  tama  n 
i  d-ufrareɣ,  ttwaliɣ-ten  dima 
yigellilen, 
ttwaḍelmen,  dɣa  ttnadiɣ  ɣef  tsebbiwin  i  ten-yewwin 
mebla lebɣi-nsen ɣer wanɣa. Ineḍliben d yimakaren, awer 
ffɣen  seg  ṭṭlam  n  bu-yikurdan.  Maca  wehmeɣ  mliḥ  mi 
bdiɣ  taɣuri  n  yikaramen  iɣef  xeddmeɣ  akked  Si  Nasser. 
Cfiɣ asmi ɣucceɣ fell-as mi yeṭṭef yiwen n uwezlu n yiwen 
n usekran i yenɣan kraḍ n yiɛeggalen n yiwet n twacult : 
ababat, tameṭṭut-is d mmi-tsen n mraw n yiseggasen  deg 
yiwen n ubaxix n ubrid. Yegla-d s usgujel n kraḍ n warrac 
meẓẓiyet deg laɛmer. Nniɣ-as i Si Nasser : 
—Amek  i  tqebleḍ  ad  tḥuddeḍ 
yessengren tawacult s lekmal-is ? 
  Yerra-yi-d : 
—Ayɣer ur t-tettḥuduɣ ara ? 
—Acku  d  aneḍlib.  Mi  inehher  tuɣ-it  d  asekran,  yernu 
ɛlaḥsab  aneqqis  n  yimsulta,  ṭumubil-ines    tella  tettazzal 
mliḥ,  ur  tquder  ara  asaḍuf,  am  wakken  ur  teḥbis  ara  ɣer 
usɣal  n  yibeddi  dɣa  tewwet  ṭumubil  n  twacult-agi  i 
yewwḍen laɛfu n Rebbi. Ɣef waya, skecmen-t ɣer lḥebs seg 
laɛḍil ad iɛeddi deg ccraɛ. 
—Tenniḍ ihi yessenger tawacult… Llan aṭas n yinehharen, 
ur  llin  ara  d  isekranen,  xedmen  ibaxixen  gellun-d  ula  d 
nutni s ungar n waṭas n twaculin, maca ɣas akken ur ten-
skecmen ara ɣer lḥebs, ur ten-urdin s wanɣa. Maca mi ara 
nwali  igemmaḍ,  ad  ten-naf  kif-kif-iten :  timenɣiwt  n 
yimdanen imeɣban,  ulac acu xedmen. 

 
 
- 66 - 

 

—Maca ameddekkel-nneɣ tuɣ-it d asekran. Yernu yeẓra s 
wacu tgellu tenhart ma yesker umdan. 
—D  acu  n  umgired  yellan  gar  tmasit  n  usekṛan-agi  d 
tmasit n unehhar ur neḥbis ara sdat n tafat tazaggaɣt,  dɣa 
yenɣa albaɛḍ ? Anehhar-agi ula d netta yeẓra yella umihi 
ma  ur  yeḥbis  ara  sdat  n  tafat  tazeggaɣt  neɣ  ma  yezger  i 
ujerriḍ awraɣ deg yimekwan uḍyiqen. 
—D tidet ayen i d-teqqareḍ. 
—Ɣas  akken,  imsulta  ad  ḍeggren  amezwaru  deg  lḥebs, 
maca wis sin ulac acu ad as-xedmen, ad yuɣal s axxam-is. 
  Ur  ufiɣ  ara  acu  ad  as-rreɣ.  Yerna  Si  Nasser  ikemmel 
deg wawal-is : 
—D  inɣiyen  n  tallit  tatiknuluǧit,  ar  tura  mazal  ur  tt-yefri 
ara  usaḍuf  yid-sen.  Anɣi  deg  usaḍuf  icudd  ɣer  nniya  n 
win i t-ixedmen, ma yella s tidet yebna ɣef ccer, mačči ɣer 
yiqurar swyes igellu. S unamek niḍen, ma yella baɛmada i 
t-yexdem. Win ara yewwten albaɛḍ s ujenwi yettwaḥseb d 
aneḍlib,  acku  yenwa  ad  yuqem  ccer,  ma  yella  d  abaxix  n 
ṭumubil,  ulac  nniya-nni  n  ccer  deg  lasel.  D  acu  ara  as-
nexdem ihi ? D wagi i d ugur n teɣdemt, ama i unezzarfu 
neɣ i umastan. 
—Tigawin  n  umdan  ddsent,  kersent,  yewɛer  fell-aneɣ  ad 
tent-nefreq s sshala gar  lxir d ccer. 
  Teɣli-d tsusmi gar-aneɣ kra n lweqt, sakin yesseqsa-yi-
d Si Nasser : 
—Ɣur-k keččini, d acu-tt tawuri n umastan ? 
—Ad iḥudd ɣef wid yettuḍelmen. 
—Kečč d arumansi, iban teɣriḍ « Victor Hugo ».

  Nniɣ-as s unecraḥ :

tewɛer. 
—Ɣriɣ  tasuqilt-ines  ɣer  taɛrabt,  d  ungal  i  d-yeffɣen  deg 
tmurt n Lubnan. 
—Ah…  Lmuhim  ilaq  ad  teẓreḍ  belli  tawuri  n  umastan  d

ɣef yineḍliben mačči d aɛǧab i aɣ-yeɛǧeb wayen i yexdem. 
Anamek  n  uḥuddu,  d  tikci  i  win  yellan  deg  lḥebs  yakk 
allalen i as-ilaqen akken ad iḥudd ɣef yiman-is, acku acḥal

i yexdem d tidet s ttbut, ad yawi tarrut ɛlaḥsab asaḍuf. 
  Akka i uɣaleɣ d amastan. D zzher i yi-yeldin tiwwura 
ɣer twuri-agi.

  Nabil,  nemḍel-it  ass-a  umbaɛd  taẓallit  n  lɛesr.  Aṭas  i

k-yessuffɣen  laɛqel.  Deg  tallit-agi  i  tselleḍ  imdanen

Banen-iyi-d d iberraniyen. Muqqleɣ ɣer kra n wudmawen

Afɣanistan. Hatta tiyita n udfel s aqerruy-iw i yi-yesfaqen. 
Amek i yi-truḥ tidet-agi. Ḥemdeɣ Yakuc mi yeɣleq Racid 
ɣef  yiman-is  yakk  tiwwura,  tili  atan  irekkem  seg  wurfan,

iberraniyen-nni  ad  kemmlen  abrid-nsen  s  tazzla,  nekk

kemmleɣ  abrid-iw  s  laɛqel  kan,  uggadeɣ  ad  ccḍeɣ  deg

  Ussan-agi  ineggura,  zgiɣ  deg  tmqebrin.    Ad  yester 
Rebbi…  Ur  ḥemmleɣ  ara  ad  beddreɣ  ayen  n  dir.  D  yir 
lfal ! Iḍelli kan neḥḍer i tenṭelt n sin seg seddis n yimsulta

Wiyaḍ,  wwin-ten  ɣer  tudrin-nsen  akken  ad  ten-meḍlen. 
Timeqbert teččur s yiselsa tizegzawin d leslaḥ. Kra kan seg

ssinen.  Ɣer  tuget  n  lmumnin,  d  lwaǧeb  am  wakken  tella

azlen ɣer tmeqbert i d-yezgan tura deg tlemmast, umbaɛd 
mi  tt-ttuɣ  ɣef  rrif  n  Ɛin-el-kerma  asmi  tella  d  tameẓyant.

Ɣer 

  Maca  ass-a,  wehmeɣ  mi  ur  ten-walaɣ  ara  deg  tenṭelt. 
Yenna-yi-d  umastan  Buɛlam  Seɛdun,  iwumi  ssawalen 
yimidawen-is  takubanit  n  Buɛlam  i  yisallen,  acku  ulac

lfetwa-agi ? Ẓran irkelli wid i tt-yessuffɣen, maca ulac win 
i izemren ad ten-yessenzen.  
 
tenṭelt,  ssuffɣen  kra  n  yimsulta 
taggara  n 
timeẓyanin-nsen, bdan tiyita n rrsas ɣer yigenni. D tiririt n 
ttar i bɣan ad sbeggnen s tigawt-agi neɣ d tuggdi i ran ad 
snejlin  seg  wulawen-nsen ?  Udmawen-nsen  berrikit  seg 
wurfan,  allen-nsen  ččurent  s  ddɣel  d  lbeɣḍ.  Beggsen  i 
umennuɣ. Qrib i d-tuɣal tmeqbert-nni d annar i uselmed n 
usemres n leslaḥ, amer ur yessekcem ara iman-is yiwen n 
ufesyan  i  yerran  talast  i  lkarnafal-agi.  Rriḥa  n  lbarud 
tɛeṭṭel  deg  yinzaren-nneɣ.  Iban  ur  yaɛǧib  ara  lḥal  i 
yimsulta  imi  d  iserdasen  i  iḍefren  imzernanen  i  sen-
irewlen. Si Aḥmed yella ɣef uqerru n wid yerfan. Azekka-
nni tameddit, mi d-ruḥeɣ ɣur-s s axxam n yimsulta, akken 
ad  waliɣ acu  i  as-yeḍran i Yusef  Ɛeyyaci  win i ttḥudduɣ, 
yenna-iyi-d llan kra n yisallen i d-yeqqaren yakk imeḥbas 
rewlen  anagar  yiwen  ufan-t  yettwajreḥ  dɣa  wwin-t  ɣer 
ssbiṭar.  Xemmemeɣ  ad  ruḥeɣ  ɣer  ssbiṭar,  maca  ẓriɣ

acku  yettuɣal  d  inigi  ayiwan,  ḥala  netta  i  izemren  ad  as-
yinin d acu yeḍran s tidet. Ḥala ameddakkel-iw Si Aḥmed 
i  yi-d-yegran  akken  ad  iyi-yefk  isallen  i  ḥwaǧeɣ.  Ruḥeɣ

Ɣef waya tejmeɛ-iyi yid-s yiwet n tdukkli d yiwet n teflest

usexdem.  Maca  nnmara  n  wat-iččumar  yessewhem-iyi 
mliḥ.  Iḍarren-nsen  ẓẓan  deg  waluḍ  armi  d  tigecrar,  kra 
deg-sen tuɣ-iten ḥafi, ttḍeggiren akal daxel n uxjiḍ mebla 
ma  yuli-asen  ula  yiwen  n  wawal.  Ulac  win  ara  iserrḥen  i 
ufus n ugelzim seg  yiḍuḍan-is armi s bessif.  Senndeɣ  ɣef 
yiwet  n  txerrubt,  kemmleɣ  amuqel  deg-sen,  wehmeɣ. 
Sugneɣ  iman-iw  deg  tlemmast  n  waluḍ-nni  s  uselsu  d 
ussebbaḍ-inu i yumsen irkelli. Ur yi-yaɛǧib ara maḍi ayen 
sugneɣ  dɣa  sefḍeɣ-t  seg  wallaɣ-iw  am  wakken  lliɣ 
xeddmeɣ asmi i yi-tuɣ d aselmad. Deg taggara, mi sersen 
ccahed  ɣef  uẓekka,  zzin-as,  ɣran  taldayt  neɣ  lfatiḥa  ɣef 
terwiḥt-is,  sakin  uɣalen  am  wakken  i  d-usan,  s  tuffra.  Ur 
ruḥen  ara  ad  walin  baba-s  n  umerḥum  am  wakken 
xedmen tuget seg wid i d-yusan ad wajhen, zzin-as-d ɣas 
akken yekkat ugeffur.  
  Mɛanaqen  s  temɣawla,  mbaddalen  kra  n  tenfaliyin  i 
susruyen s laɛqel, yal yiwen seg yirgazen yuɣal seg wansi

ssneɣ  d  acu  iwumi  ssawalen    lbenna  n  tɣuri.  Ur  lliɣ  ara 
seg  wid  iḥemmlen  uraren  n  lkarṭa,  ɣas  ma  yella  tuget  n 
yinelmaden  n  tesnawit  sɛeddayen  acḥal  n  sswayeɛ  deg 
wurar  s uɛeggeḍ, ama daxel n yisganen neɣ deg lawan n 
usgunfu  deg  tɣemmar  n  umraḥ  neɣ  daxel  n  tneɣriyin 
tilmawin. Ttkeyyifen, ttnaɣen, ttawin-d awal ɣef wayen n 
dir-i,  tikkwal  ttuɣalen  ɣer  yifassen  d  rrkel  akken  ad  frun 
lxilaf  d  lemgarda  yellan  gar-asen.  Griɣ  tamkerḍit  d 
ugerruj ur nfennu i teffer. Ɣliɣ s ugacur ɣef kra n yidlisen 
n  « Albert  Camus »  yenna-d  deg-sen  d  akken  aflusuf 
almani  « Nietzche »  ur  yenɣi  ara  Yakuc,  acku  aneggaru-a 
aṭas aya segmi yemmut. Tafyirt-a teɣli-d fell-i am tirmegt 
neɣ  rrɛud.  D  acu-ten  yimeslayen-agi ?  Amek  ad  yemmet 
win  yellan  d  ameɣlal ?  D  tafyirt-agi  i  yi-yewwin  ɣer 
teflusuft  n  « Nietzche »,  sakin  ɣer  « Karl  Marx »  akked 
« Siegmnund  Freud ».  Ɣliɣ  imir-n  ɣef  yidlisen  n  teflusuft, 
bdiɣ ttxemmimeɣ ɣef tikti-a n tmettant n Yakuc d wamek i 
yexdem  umdan  akken  ad  yaɣ  amkan-is  deg  lqaɛa.  Yakuc 
swayes  numen  d  tmeɣlelt-ines,  win  i  nettaggad  tarrut  d 
unazir-ines, yuɣal d tikti i yesnulfa umdan yettidiren deg 
tallit  taqburt  akken  ad  yessegzi  tuggdi-ines  seg  tumanin 
tigamanin.  Tressa  tekti  deg  wallaɣ-iw,  thucc  tigensas-inu 
timezwura.  Lliɣ  ḥemmleɣ  mliḥ  idlisen  n  teflusuft,  ɣef 
waya  ɣriɣ 
iqdimen  d 
idlisen  n  yimussnawen-ines, 
yimaynuten,  seg  Aflaṭun  armi  « Camus »  d  « Sartre », 
mebla ma ttuɣ « Hiegel », « Marks », « Freud » d « Herbert 
Markus ». Yezzi-d fell-i uqusis, ur zemireɣ ad ffɣeɣ seg-s.

Yernu ur cukkeɣ ara ad d-yas wass  ad as-ffɣeɣ. Umbaɛd 
n  taggazt  n  uselmed  i  teẓriḍ,  d  lbakalurya  i  d-wwiɣ  deg 
tegnatin  tidinkuciṭin,  skelseɣ  iman-iw  deg  tneɣrit  n 
teflusuft, maca tasertit tamcumt teskerker-iyi nekk mazal-
iyi  d  ameẓyan,  deg  yiwet  n  tallit  ḥesbeɣ  iman-iw  d 
Lmehdi  i  tettraǧu  talsa,  win  ara  ibeddlen  amaḍal  s 
usunded  neɣ  tamesbanit  n  yinelmaden.  D  taḥkayt 
taɣezzfant, ahat ad d-yas wass ad k-tt-id-alseɣ s telqi. 
  Yessusem  umeddakkel-iw,  yeɣreq  deg  yiwet  n  tsusmi 
ad  as-tiniḍ  deg  tenṭelt  i  yella.  Qudreɣ  leḥzen-ines,  ur  t-
hewwjeɣ  ara  s  yiseqsiyen-inu.  Deg  uzal-nni  nruḥ  ad 
nmerreḥ  deg  tmersit.  Sḥebseɣ  ṭumubil  sdat  n  ugenna  n 
yiɣerruba  n  useggeḍ  anda  llan  kraḍ  neɣ  ukkuẓ  n 
yilmeẓyen  ttɛummun  s  zzux  d  uɛeggeḍ  deg  waman 
yumsen, sekkren ahruḥu. Nniɣ-as i Racid ad nsew taqbuct 
n lbira neɣ snat ɣer umeddakkel-nneɣ Lǧilali, maca ihuzz 
aqerruy-is  akken  ad  iyi-yini  ala.  Akka  i  yettwaxdem 
Racid,  iɣelleq  ɣef  yiman-is,  ma  yeqber  wul-is,  yettsusum. 
Maca  ẓriɣ  irekkem  daxel-is,  acku  walaɣ  ifassen-is  amek  i 
ttergigin  mi  ara  yebdu  ameslay  ddaw  n  tuɣmest.  Mi  d-
nuɣal, aṭas i mmeslayeɣ, nniɣ-as akk ayen sɛiɣ d nnhayat 
limmer ad ssifsusent fell-as taẓayt n twaɣit i yeɣlin fell-as. 
Sakin,  mebla  ma  xemmemeɣ,  bdiɣ  ameslay,  i  tikkelt 
tamezwarut, ɣef  lḥif n ledwar tineggura n baba.  
  Yal  tikkelt  mi  ara  d-mmektiɣ  tadyant-agi,  yettneqbaḍ 
wul-iw,  kerrheɣ  tudert-iw.  Atemmu-nni  yettulsen  ideg 
yeṭṭef  baba tasga. Yiwet n tsusmi yessaggaden yemmɣen 
ɣef wadeg-nni, ḥala tusut taqesḥant n baba i tt-igezzmen.

yenɛel Rebbi daɣen ! Ayɣer i nruḥ ɣer ṭṭaleb-nni aberkan,

  Yir  ccfawat  ttnernit,  ta  nnig  tayeḍ,  skecment  deg  wul-

usaru ara iyi-isettun imira-inu d yizri-inu  armi i yi-tewwi 
tnafa. 
 
Seg uzal-nni yugi ad iyi-yeṭṭixer yiwen n useqsi : d acu-
tt  taḥkayt-agi  taqdimt  i  yerran  tameṭṭut  n  Racid  ad  tɣil 
aṭṭan i tt-yuɣen d tarrut ɣef yiwet n sseyya i texdem yiwen 
n  wass ?  D  acu-tt  sseyya-agi ?  Ameddakkel-iw  yettwali-tt 
d taḥkayt taqdimt tɣumm-itt tatut aṭas aya. Iban, Racid ur

yettwali  ara  sseyya-agi  am  wakken  i  tt-twali  tmeṭṭut-is, 
mgaradent tmuɣliwin-nsen. 
  Deg ddurt-nni ttwaṭṭfeɣ qrib yal ass s temliliyin akken 
ad nwali amek ad nḥudd ɣef yimeɣnasen isertiyen i teṭṭef

umraḥ n umenzu n Mayyu akken ad bedden mgal tuṭṭfa n

uɣmis  afransiss  ideg  yenna  belli  anagraw  n  tmurt  yenɣa 
yiwen  seg  yizumal  n  temgadla  berra  n  tmurt.  Nuɣ 
tannumi  nettemlili  deg  tnarit  n  umastan  Si  Nasser, 
nettnadi  ɣef  yikalan  iwulmen  akken  ad  nexdem  akken 
iwulem. 
  D  wagi  i  yi-d-yeǧǧan  ad  ttuɣ  maḍi  taḥkayt  n  Racid  d 
waṭṭan n tmeṭṭut-is ; ur ruḥeɣ ad ten-ẓureɣ, ur seqsaɣ ɣef 
liḥala-nsen snat n ledwar. Ur ẓriɣ ara d acu i yi-yesmektan 
yis-s  mi  lliɣ  tetteɣ  imekli  akked  yiwen  n  umidaw  deg 
usečču  i  iqublen  axxam  n  teɣdemt.  Ahat  d  tamectarit-nni 
yettaken  anzi  ɣer  tmeṭṭut  n  umeddakkel-iw  i  yeqqimen 
lmendad-iw.  Refdeɣ  kan  aqerruy-iw  ɣef  yiḍebsiyen  armi 
ɣlint wallen-iw fell-as. Tfaq ttmuquleɣ deg-s, ur as-yaɛǧib 
ara  lḥal,  tekker  tbeddel  amkan.  Sḥisfeɣ  snat  n  tikkal. 
Tamezwarut, mi hewwjeɣ massa-nni, nekk ur lliɣ ara seg 
wid  yettazzalen  deffir  n  tlawin.  Tis  snat,  ɣef  ustehzi-inu. 
Amek i iruḥ Racid seg wallaɣ-iw snat n ledwar yernu ẓriɣ 
tameṭṭut-is tuḍen mliḥ. Dɣa ṭṭfeɣ rray ad seɣtiɣ lɣelṭa-inu. 
—S tmara i tt-skecmeɣ ɣer ssbiṭar.

ad qellben amek ad inigen ɣas ɣer unazir… ur qebbleɣ ara

yizerfan-iw  am  yizem,  maca  ur  rekḍeɣ  ara  izerfan  n 
wiyaḍ.

Banen-d  urfan  ɣef  wudem  n  Nasira  i  iɣilen  d  Racid  ur

Nasira  ad  teṭṭef  amkan  i  d-yusan  deffir  n  unehhar.

Amkan-nni ttwalint-t yakk wid yellan deg lkar, ur yezmir

uxxam n umeddakkel-is Zubir. Tenna-as tmeṭṭut-is : 
—Uqbel  ma  txedmeḍ  kra,  ilaq  ad  tẓer  Nasira  ma  tella  s

umussu n temɣuzla, txeddem deg ssbiṭar n Bab El-Wad. 
—U ma yella s tadist i tella, d acu ara nexdem ? 
—Ur zewwir ara temsal… Yal tamsalt deg lawan-is. 
  Yesserwes  Racid  lweqt  n  tgannit  akken  ad  d-ffɣen

yimeddukkal-nsen. Yernu yiwen n wass tenna-as-t-id deg

tameɣra tameqqrant, am nitni am yimaɛcaq irkelli. Tban-d

Baba-s  am  leɛwayed-is  ijemmeɛ  arraw-is,  asmi  llan  d 
imeẓyanen, deffir-is akken ad ẓallen. Racid yeḥbes taẓallit 
segwasmi  yeffeɣ  seg  uxxam  akken  ad  iɣer.  Yal  tikkelt

weḥd-s. Maca yiwet n tikkelt, iqubel-it baba-s s tidet : 
—Ẓriɣ  tḥebseḍ  taẓallit…  yaxi  teẓriḍ  win  i  yettaǧǧan 
taẓallit  ɣur-neɣ  yettwaḥsab  d  amṭurni,  d  akafriw.  Nekk, 
ur bɣiɣ ara ad yili mmi d akafriw, acku taggara-s d anazir, 
ad aɣ-yenǧu Rebbi. Ɣef waya,  aql-ik sdat sin n yiberdan : 
ama  ad  d-tuɣaleḍ  ɣer  laɛqel-ik,  dɣa  ad  d-tuɣaleḍ  ɣer 

 
 
- 124 - 

 

tẓallit am keččini am watmaten-ik, neɣ kečč mačči d mmi, 
ur k-ssineɣ ara, ternuḍ učči-inu d leḥram fell-ak. 
  Racid  yerfa,  ibedd  deg  wudem  n  baba-s  i  yeḥseb    d 
ameqqal.  Yenna-as 
lǧennet  d  unazir  d  asnulfu  n 
yimdanen,  ur  sɛin  ara  assaɣ  d  tidet.  Baba-s  yerfa  mliḥ, 
yessaɛseq-it seg uxxam. Seg wass-nni, ur  d-yuɣal Racid s 
axxam  n  yimawlan-is ḥala  snat  n  tikkal,  yeqqim  deg-sent 
kra  n  tsaɛtin  kan,  iqesser  deg-sent  akked  yemma-s  d  kra 
seg  watmaten-is.  Deg  yal  tikkelt,  tessuter  deg-s  yemma-s 
ad  yessuter  ssmaḥ  seg  baba-s,  tuɣ-it  yerfa  mi  as-ffɣen 
wawalen-nni,  yernu  asumer-ines  d  aggaz  kan,  iɣil  ad 
yuɣal ɣer laɛqel-is. Ur ixemmem ara irkelli ad yeǧǧ axxam 
i  lebda.  Deg  tẓallit-ines,  yezga  ideɛɛu-as  s  tuɣalin  ɣer 
ubrid amaɣud. 
  Amek  ad  yuɣal  s  axxam  umbaɛd  n  yiba  n  ukkuẓ  n 
yiseggasen  neɣ  ugar,  mačči  d  tujjma  i  ten-yejjem,  d 
lemzeyya  ad  sen-yessuter :  ad  as-xeḍben  tameṭṭut.  Ad 
ikellex i uḍeggal-is ? Ad yawi yid-s kra seg yimeddukkal-
is d yiwet n temɣart ara yestaɛemlen iman-is d yemma-s d 
yiwen  n  umɣar  ara  yerren  iman-is  d  baba-s ?  Ugur  atan 
deg  Racid,  ur  iḥemmel  tamaɛmult,  ur  iḥemmel  astaɛmel. 
Deg yiwen n wass deg wussan n Rebbi, yeṭṭef lkar, yuɣal 
ɣer  taddart-is.  Tmuger-it-id  yemma-s  s  yimeṭṭawen  d 
tuzzma.  Seddis  n  wagguren  mi  yewweḍ  baba-s  laɛfu  n 
Rebbi, yemmut umbaɛd aṭṭan i t-yuɣen kra n ledwar. Ulac 
acu i as-nnan, acku baba-s yugi maḍi, yenna-asen urǧin ad 
yessuref  i  win  ad  t-ixebbren,  la  deg  ddunit  wala  deg 
laxert.  Yefren umelɛun abrid-is, ad iḍebber aqerruy-is ihi.

Ṭṭaɛa  n  yimawlan  d  lferḍ  deg  usɣan-nneɣ,  yeṭṭef  amkan

temmeslayeḍ  ɣef  mmi-k.  D  acu  tessneḍ  fell-as ?  Ɣef

n  yimsulta  ad  tqelleb  deg  leḥwayej-is,  ahat  yeǧǧa  kra  n 
warraten  ara ɣ-yalen deg tsestant-nneɣ. 
  Yessider  Racid i uqerruy-is, yenna-d ddaw n teɣmest : 
« D ahdum, d tawaɣit … ɣer taggara n laɛmer-iw ad yuɣal 
mmi d arebrab … axxam-iw d aglat n yirebraben… ». 

 
 
- 134 - 

 

Skecmeɣ iman-iw, nniɣ-asen : 

—Mačči d wagi i d-nenna. Nebɣa ad nwali amek i tewweḍ

deg-k ad aɣ-tɛiwneḍ. 
 
—A  Si  Aḥmed,  ssneɣ  tawacult  n  Racid  aṭas  n  yiseggasen 
aya, ur cukkeɣ ara tesɛa assaɣ d yineḍliben-agi. 
—Anwa  i  yerdan  tawacult  s  lḥaǧa ?  Nettmeslay  kan  ɣef 
mmi-tsen  yemmuten,  yewwḍen  laɛfu  n  Rebbi.  Ayen 
nebɣa d isallen ara ɣ-yessawḍen ɣer wid yenɣan amsaltu. 
Ayen yaɛnan tameẓyant, d lxiḍ ayiwan i nla imir-a. Yallah 
a Si Racid mmeslay-d… 
  Umbaɛd n tsusmi taẓayant, yenna-d ukumisar : 
—Hder-iyi-d  ɣef  yimeddukkal  n  mmi-k ?  Bɣiɣ  ad  d-iniɣ 
imeddukkal-is seg wat-yiččumar. 
—Imeddukkal at-yiččumar ? Ur ten-ssineɣ, ur bɣiɣ ad ten-
issineɣ. 
—S laɛqel kan… xemmem ciṭuḥ … ahat… 
  Yessider Racid i uqerruy-is, ixemmem kra n tsanin : 
—Ah, d tidet… yella yiwen d awezzlan, d imsibrek mliḥ, 
yelsa  tacacit  d  ubalṭu  nnig  n  uqendur.  Walaɣ-t  yiwen  n 
ubrid  ibedd  sdat  n  tewwurt  n  uɣerbaz  alemmas.  Ad  tili 
ssaɛa qrib d setta n tmeddit. Seqsaɣ-t acu yeḥwaǧ. Yenna-
yi-d  yettraǧu  deg  Nabil.  Imuqel-iyi-d  ddaw  n  tiṭ,  am 
wakken tella lḥaǧa deg wul-is. Tameddit-nni seqsaɣ mmi 
fell-as.  Yenna-yi-d :  d  ameddakkel-iw.  Nniɣ-as :  yeqqar 
yid-k  deg  tesdawit ?  Yenna-yi-d :  ulac  acu  i  k-yaɛnan,  d 
ameddekkel-iw, d aya ! 
—Melmi teḍra temlilit-agi ?

ineslem ».  Nniɣ-ak :  wagi  mačči  d  aselsu  n  yinselmen,  d

tmurt  n  Yifɣaniyen.  Inselmen  mzerbɛen  deg  umaḍal,  yal

nessawal ineslem, maca yella uselsu axaliǧi, irani, amalizi,

d  izenẓaren  n  yiṭij  n  tnezzayt.  Negzeɣ  ad  ldiɣ  tawwurt. 
Yenna-d s uqesser : 
—Tegganem akked tyuẓaḍ tura ? 
  Yettbin-d deg uselsu-ines n userdas am umnay izedɣen 
tirga-inu.  Yessers  tabalizt-ines  tameqqrant  ɣef  umnar  n 
tewwurt,  nemsalam  s  yiwet  n  leḥrara  yesseḥmayen 
ulawen. Yufeg  leḥzen, iruḥ ṭṭlam d tsusmi n utemmu. 

 
 
- 150 - 

 

—Yesseɛya-yi yinig,  yernu laẓ igezzem iẓerman-iw. 
  Tenna-d yemma s ciṭuḥ n leḥya : 
—Ur  neẓri  ara  ad  d-taseḍ  ass-a  a  Lmilud  a  mmi…  nečča 
ayen d-yegran … maca ssber kan rrbeɛ n ssaɛa, ad kreɣ ad

—Ur ssaɛyu ara iman-im a yemma. Wwiɣ-awen-d imensi 
izad.  Amek  ad  d-uɣaleɣ  s  axxam  umbaɛd  leɣyab  n  sin  n 
wagguren s yifassen d ilmawen ? 
  Yeldi  tabalizt,  yessufeɣ-d  seg-s  ḥala  lqut  yelhan : 
aɣrum  n  ubulunji,  d  amellal,  tayaẓiḍt  yewwan  mazal-itt 
akken teḥma, aguglu, azemmur, ččina, taqarɛet n lgazuz d 
lḥelwa  n  « mille  feuilles ».  Nessaɣ-d  tacemmaɛt  niḍen, 
neččur ṭṭabla s wučči-nni aẓiḍan, neqqim nettqessir, urǧin 
neqqim tiɣimit am ta. 
  Yessuffeɣ-d sakin iselsa imaynuten i ɣ-d-yewwi i nekk 
d  yemma.  Lsiɣ-ten  s  zzux,  suguneɣ  iman-iw  leḥḥuɣ  deg 
yiberdan  n  taddart,  aqerruy-iw  deg  yigenni,  tikkelt-a  ur 
ttsetḥiɣ  ara s yiselsa-inu, mačči d iqdimen-nni yeččuren s 
tfawtin  deg  tgecrar  neɣ  deffir  n  userwal-iw.  Iḍ-nni,  ṭṭseɣ 
yis-sen  s  tumert,  ḥulfaɣ  i  yiman-iw  d  afug  i  ttafgeɣ  ɣef 
usigna  i  yetthuzu  yiwen  n  waḍu  d  afessas.  Yeqqim  gma 
yid-neɣ  mraw  n  wussan.  I  tikkelt  tamezwarut,  mi  ara  d-

d  tebwaḍin  n  leḥelwa  n  ssenf  n  « biscuit ».  Mi  d-nuɣal,

—Anda tesliḍ i yimeslayen-agi ay amcum ?

Susmeɣ,  kkreɣ  ffɣeɣ.  Ɛemmi  Muḥ  ttqadaren-t  yirkelli.

awal-iw  a mmi. 
 
Ur yettmeslay ara aṭas, maca awalen-is weznen d ureɣ.

yirgazen. » Tuɣal tettenkar zik, tettruḥu ɣer utemmu-nneɣ 
aqdim, tqelleɛ awri weḥd-s kan, tettaǧǧa-t din, mi zrin kra

laɛqel kan ɣer uxxam-nneɣ i d-yezgan deg taddart.

d tmenya. Dɣa ttɣamayeɣ ass s lekmal-is mebla ccɣel. Kra

akumisar  n  temsulta,  ad  as-yales  kulci.  Maca,  mi 
nxemmem mliḥ nufa asummer-agi ur iwulem ara. Kraḍ n 
yimsulta  ad  bedden  mgal-nneɣ.  Awal-nsen  mgal  awal-
nneɣ. Ugar n waya, isɣunen yellan ɣer gma deg tḥanut d 
anza  mgal-is.  D  ayen  yenɣa-t  ccreɛ.  Neɣli  deg  yiwen  n 
uwaɣiw  ameqqran,  ur  neẓri  ara  amek  ad  nefsi  lexyuḍ-is. 
Yeṭṭef Karim rray ad yessenz isɣunen-nni ɣer wid yessen 
seg  yiḥeddaden  neɣ  imsenza  n  wureɣ  ur  nesɛi  lekwaɣeḍ 
yettilin  deg  kra  n  yizenqan  n  tmanaɣt.  Kraḍ  n  wussan  d 
tazzla deg leswaq-nni uffiren. Sselɛa teɣleb imsaɣen. Ureɣ 
ur yettnuz ara s sshala, labaɛda win yettwaxedmen yakan, 
win  ur  nesɛi  ara  ṭṭabeɛ  neɣ  win  ur  nesɛi  tifaṭurin  i  ɣ-d-
yemmalen seg wansi i d-yusa. Iqelleb daɣen ɣef tenmeslin 
n yiḥeddaden akken ad sen-yessenz isɣunen i usefsi-nsen 
iwakken ad sen-ɛiwden ṣṣenɛa s wadda. Maca ur yufi ara 
amsaɣ  ɣas  ssuma-nnsen  rxiset.  Am  wakken  yeṭṭuqet 
unadi  deg  tserglin  n  yimsulta  i  d-yennernan  s  waṭas,

sin yid-sen. Wis sin mazal-it yedder. Sɣur-s ad yekk ccer.

Buɛebdellah.  Bedden  yirgazen-nni  ɣef  umnar  n  tewwurt, 
ur  kcimen  ara  daxel.  Walan  kan  Karim,  yeṭṭef-it  yiwen  n 
umsaltu  seg  yiɣil,  ad  as-tiniḍ  yessen-it  yakan,  idegger-it 
daxel n ṭumubil, yesrugmet kra n waggazen. Yewweḍ-iyi-
d  lexbar  tanezzayt  n  uzekka-nni.  Imir-n  kan  faqeɣ, 
takerḍa-ines ur tesɛi ara assaɣ d umennuɣ mgal n rrebrab 
am  wakken  i  d-qqaren,  acku  ad  qellben  fell-i  ula  d  nekk. 
Ma  d  Karim,  d  amsenzu  n  wureɣ  yebɛed  mliḥ  ɣef 
umennuɣ aserti. Ayɣer ad t-ddmen deg yiḍ ? Ɣef temsulta 
ad truḥ kan ɣer tḥanut-is ideg yettɣimi s ṭul n wass, wa ad 
t-tawi  sdat  n  medden.  Maca  ur  texdim  ara  akka,  acku 
niyya-ines  ur  tesfi  ara.  Walaɣ  baba  deg  tazwara  n  uzal, 
sutreɣ  deg-s  ad  iruḥ  ad  yesseqsi  fell-as  deg  uxxam  n 
temsulta.  Nnan-as-d  ur  ṭṭifen  ara  albaɛḍ  s  yisem-agi. 
Yuɣal-d  xayeb.  Baba  d  ameɣbun,  teqher-it  ddunit. 
Yesɛedda  ddunit-is  d  axemmas  deg 
lfirmat,  yettaɣ 
tajernaḍt  tamecṭuḥt  maḍi.  Anagar  taɣiwant  i  yessen  seg 
tedbelt. Ɣef waya ulac acu i d-yenna i umsaltu i as-yennan 
ur sḥebsen ara albaɛḍ s yisem i  yebder.  Ukkuẓ  n  wussan 
umbaɛd, usan-d yimsulta deg ṭumubil tunsibt ɣer uxxam-
nneɣ,  ɣef  lɛecra  n  ssbeḥ,  ttnadin  ɣef  Karim  Buɛebdellah, 
amsenzu  n  wureɣ.  Ḥala  yemma  i  yellan  deg  uxxam. 
Tenna-asen, mmi-s Karim atan d ameḥbus ɣur-sen, tusa-d 
temsulta tewwi-t deg yiḍ. Deg tazwara yewhem umsaltu-
nni,  sakin  yenna-as,  temsulta  ur  tettawi  ara  imdanen  deg 
yiḍ,  ḥala  ma  llan  d  ineḍliben  imerwalen.  Yessefhem-as 
ttnadin  ɣef  Ɛebdelkrim  Buɛebdellah,  d  aḥeddad  n  lfeṭṭa 
deg  tlemmast  n  temdint.  Ruḥen  deg  tazwara  ɣer  tḥanut-

ines, maca ufan-tt teɣleq, dɣa usan-d ad nadin fell-as deg 
uxxam-is.  Ḥwaǧen-t  deg  yiwet  n  tsestant  ɣef  tkurḍa  n 
yisɣunen.  Tenna-asen  yemma  i  tikkelt  tis  snat,  tusa-d 
yakan yiwet n terbeɛt n temsulta am nitni deg tlemmast n 
yiḍ,  tewwi-t  yid-s.  Seg  yiḍ-nni,  ur  iban  ara  lexbar-is. 
Amsaltu-nni  yeǧǧa-as  kan  taseɣra  ɣef  yisem  n  gma, 
yenna-as  yessefk  fell-as  ad  iruḥ  s  temɣawla  ɣer  uxxam  n 
temsulta.  Yemma,  ur  tefhim  acemma.  Mi  ruḥeɣ  ad  tt-
waliɣ  deg  yiḍ-nni,  ufiɣ-tt  tettwanɣeḍ,  ur  teḥbis  ara  seg 
yimeṭṭawen.  Anwa-ten  wigi  i  yewwin  Karim  ma  mačči  d 
imsulta ? Tamsulta tebḍa d tirebbuyaɛ. Wid i d-yusan deg 
uzal  ttgensisen  tuddsa  tunsibt.  Ma  d  iminigen  n  yiḍ, 
ttekkan  deg  terebbuyaɛ  iwumi  ssawalen  tirebbuyaɛ  n 
umennuɣ mgal rrebrab i ṭṭafaren taɣellist taserdasant. Deg 
tnezzayt  n  uzekka-nni,  tuɣal-d  tarbaɛt-nni  s  timmad-is, 
tnuda yakk axxam. Ulac acu ufan. Sutren tisura n tḥanut. 
Tqelleb fell-asent deg leǧyub n yiselsa n Karim, tefka-asen 
tisura-nni.  Kra  n  tsaɛtin  umbaɛd,  uɣalen-d  s  axxam, 
wwin-d yid-sen  imsulta niḍen,  nudan-t  i tikkelt tis  snat  s 
telqi. Baba tuɣ-it deg uxxam imir-n, wwin-t yid-sen. Neẓra 
umbaɛd,  mi  nudan  taḥanut  n  Karim,  ufan  ayen  d-yegran 
seg  yisɣunen  yettwakren.  Yuɣal  gma  d  amaker  n 
yisɣunen,  neɣ  d  amɛiwen  n  yimakaren  imi  d  netta  i  ten-

Tagi  d  tazmamt  n  mmi  Nabil,  ufiɣ-tt  deg  tlemmast  n 
yidlisen-ines.  Yella  yettaru  deg-s  ayen  i  yettɛeddayen  ɣef 
uqerruy-is.  Am  wakken  teẓriḍ,  ffreɣ-tt  ɣef  temsulta.  D  Si 
Aḥmed i yeskecmen tawekka deg uqerruy-iw, dɣa uɣaleɣ-
d srid qellbeɣ taxzant-is. Teqqim texxamt-is am wakken i 
tt-yeǧǧa.  La  nekk  wala  yemma-s  ur  nesɛi  tabɣest  ad 
neqɛed  lqecc-is.  Yemma-s  tettɣimi  ɣef  umnar  n  tewwurt, 
tesmektay  ccfawat-ines  akked  tasa-ines  am  wakken  i  as-
tsemmi, ma yeqreḥ-itt mliḥ lḥal, tettaẓ asurif ɣer sdat, ad 
teṭṭef  aselsu  amezwaru  ara  d-tmager,  ad  t-tessenṭeḍ  ɣer 
wudem-is, ad tebdu sakin imeṭṭawen d unedder. Ulac acu 
ad  d-iniɣ  neɣ  ayen  zemreɣ  ad  xedmeɣ.  Ula  d  nekk  deg 
wussan  imezwura,  amer  mačči  d  tiruggza  i  yi-yefkan

  Acu  ad  xedmeɣ  s  tezmamt-agi ?  Yenna-yi-d  baba : 
« Ad k-tenfeɛ i yiluɣma n tusnakt d teɣrasna ». Tusnakt d

kulci.  Ula  d  baba  bdiɣ  kerrheɣ-t.  Ayɣer  ur  yettẓalla,  ur 
yettuẓum am netta am lbaqi n yinselmen ? Ur yuggad seg 
ssikis n uẓekka d tmes n unazir ? Deg wass n sem yezrin, 
mi  yebda  limam  amennay  igellem  deg  ssikis  n  uẓekka  d 
lɛezla  n  lmegget  d  tuggdi-ines  seg  Ɛeẓrayen,  aneglus  n 
tmettant,  u  netta  weḥd-s  kan,  isell  i  yisurifen  n  wid  i  t-
imeṭṭlen  yettenɣas  ssut-nsen,  ttbaɛden  fell-as,  tergagi 
tfekka-inu  seg  tuggdi.  Ur  kfiɣ  taẓallit-inu  armi  uɣaleɣ  d 
ulac.  Ttẓallaɣ  s  ṭul  n  yiḍ,  am  wakken  ttẓallaɣ  deg  lawan, 
steɣfireɣ  Rebbi  ssbeḥ  tameddit  akken  ad  iyi-yessuref. 
Yenna-yi-d  Yasin  Rebbi  iseffeḍ  yakk  ddnub  ma  yuɣal 
umdan  s  abrid  amaɣud.  Nettemlili  yal  ass  deg  lǧameɛ, 
deg tẓallit n lefjer akked tin n lɛica. Ssaɛa qrib ad taweḍ d 
ṭnac  n  wass.  D  lawan  ad  ruḥeɣ  ɣer  lǧameɛ  i  tẓallit  n 
lǧumuɛa. Yasin yettraǧu-iyi. Iḥettet fell-i ad n-awaḍeɣ zik 
acku  Ccix  Meḥfuḍ  ad  ɣ-d-yas  seg  Blida  akken  ad  ɣ-
yessiwel inaw n wass n lǧumuɛa. Yasin yebɣa ad neqqim 
deg lesfuf imezwura.

Aram, 18 seg furar 
  Yessuffeɣ-iyi  ass-a  uselmad  n  teɣrasna  akked  kraḍ  n

yesɛa zzher, ɣur-s daɣen tabɣest tameqqrant. Aṭas i nelḥa, 
neqqim  nettales  i  tenfaliyin  swayes  tettɛeggiḍ  yakk 
lɛamma.  (Fell-as  ad  nidir,  fell-as  ad  nemmet :  ccariɛa, 
ccariɛa  …  Ulac  tamendawt,  ulac  arakwal :  Leqran, 
Leqran…) « Igduden-a, d tazmert tameqqrant, zemren  ad 
refden  idurar  ma  numeṛ-iten  s  waya »,  am  wakken  i  d-
yenna  yiwen  seg  lmacayex  deg  yinaw-ines  deg  umraḥ  n 
yimeɣrasen.  Ass-nni  faqeɣ  mačči  weḥd-i  i  lliɣ.  Yeččur 
wul-iw  s  tumert  d  nnefxa  s  wayen  xeddmeɣ,  ɣas  ibedd 

 
 
- 211 - 

 

lxilafa  ad  tegzem 

baba deg wudem-iw. Mi d-nuɣal, yenna-yi-d Yasin  ad tili 
yiwet  n  tmesbanit  tameqqrant  niḍen  deg  wussan  i  d-
iteddun  deg  umraḥ  n  yimeɣrasen,  ad  teqqim  alamma 
sbedden  lxilafa  tineslemt.  Yernu  qrib  ad  tt-sbedden  ma 
yebɣa  Rebbi.  Ad  nefreḥ  irkelli,  wa  ad  nessenger  icenga  n 
usɣan. Xemmemeɣ ɣef taggara n baba d uletma d umkan-
nsen deg lxilafa-agi. S tidet d icenga n usɣan ? Yessefk fell-
i  ad  sqenɛeɣ  baba  ad  yeǧǧ  abrid  n  tezdukkla  wa  ad 
yekcem ɣer tneslemt. Ilaq ad xedmeɣ aya uqbel n usbeddi 
n  lxilafa.  Ur  bɣiɣ  ara  ad  yeḍru  wayen  n  dir  i  baba  d 
iqerra  n 
uletma.  Yenna-d  Yasin 
yikafriwen d tlawin mebla lḥiǧab. Ilaq ad sqenɛeɣ uletma 
akken ad d-tels lḥiǧab, wa ad teḥbes rrwaḥ-ines ɣer yillel. 
Attan  tura  deg  tesdawit.  Imuras  qrib  ad  d-awḍen,  nettat 
tuɣ tannumi tessucuf deg yillel akked yirgazen. Ya Rebbi 
all-iyi akken ad ten-rreɣ s abrid amaɣud. 
 
Aram, 11 seg yunyu 
 
Suref-as  a  Rebbi  i  baba  mi  itett  Remḍan.  Ẓriɣ  ur 
yettuẓummu  ara.  Maca  tasebḥit-agi  mi  t-walaɣ  deg 
tnawalt  itess  lqehwa-ines,  nekkni  deg  waggur  asaɛdi 
yettubarken, ur ṭṭifeɣ ara iman-iw, ɛeggḍeɣ fell-as, nniɣ-as 
kečč d akafriw, ad k-yessekcem Rebbi ɣer unazir. Ass-nni 
yennecraḥ.  Yessewhem-iyi  ass-nni,  ur  yerfi  ara  am  zik. 
Yessuter  deg-i  ad  qqimeɣ,  yebda  ad  i  yi-yessefhem 
tafelsuft-ines ur nettamnen ara s Rebbi. Iban, ur sliɣ ara i 
wayen  yettmeslay.  Ur  selleɣ  ara  i  lweswas  n  cciṭan.  D 
cciṭan amelɛun i yettmeslayen s yiles-is. Netta yettmeslay, 

 
 
- 212 - 

 

nekk  ttalseɣ  s  tsusmi  tasuret  n  « Elmuɛwidateyn ».  Sakin 
furseɣ  tagnit  mi  yessaɣ  agarru,  yeddem  afenǧal  ad  isew 
lqehwa, beddeɣ wwiɣ-d ssebba s rrwaḥ-inu ɣer tesnawit, 
ɣas akken nekfa akradyur-nneɣ, u nesɛa azref ur nḥedder 
ara i temsirin. Uggadeɣ ad as-gezmen aqerruy-is asmi ara 
tbedd lxilafa. All-iyi a Rebbi akken ad ldiɣ ul-is i sburren 
yifyar n cciṭan ! 
 
Acer, 16 seg yunyu 
  D acu-tent twuɣa-agi i iɣellin ɣef uqerruy-iw ? Deg yiḍ 
yezrin,  tuɣ-iyi  weḥd-i  deg  usalun,  qqareɣ  yiwen  n  udlis. 
Baba  d  anabay,  ulac-it  deg  uxxam.  Yenna-d  ad  iruḥ  ɣer 
Leɣwaṭ deg tirza n tesweḍt taneggarut. Uletma attan deg 
uɣrem asdawen deg tmanaɣt. Yemma teṭṭes deg texxamt-
is.  Ɛyiɣ  deg  tɣuri,  ur  nuddmeɣ  ara.  Saɣeɣ  tiliẓri,  bdiɣ 
ttbeddileɣ  deg  yimaṭṭafen  limmer  ad  afeɣ  asaru  ara 
yessedhun.  Ɛlaɣila,  thucc-iyi  yiwet  n  tugna  n  usaru  n 
wuzuf. Tameṭṭut tecbeḥ mliḥ tcerreɛ i yimessaḍen-is, tefka 
aḥeččun-is i yiwen n ubbuc ibedden ikeccem deg-s s zzur. 
Tafekka-inu teṭṭef-itt tergagayt. Yiwet n taɣect i d-yekkan 
seg  daxel-iw  tettɛeggiḍ,  teqqar-iyi-d  « d  leḥram  …  sens-
itt… sexsi-tt  »,  maca  tafekka-inu  tekref,  tugi  ad  d-terr 
awal.  Tugna-nni  teɣli-d  fell-i  am  ssiɛqa.  Urǧin  walaɣ 
tameṭṭut ɛeryan neɣ amek i ixeddem urgaz tayri i tmeṭṭut. 
Deg  kra  n  lweqt  kan  ḥulfaɣ  i  uzɣal  yettaɣ  yakk  tafekka-
inu,  ḥusseɣ  daɣen  i  ubbuc-iw  yettenkar.  Tessewhem-iyi 
tugna-nni  tareqmant  yellan  sdat  n  wallen-iw  yebrarḥen. 
Uggadeɣ ad yessaki unazeɛ n tmeṭṭut-nni yeččuren asalun

yemma. Ṭṭfeɣ « atilikumund », sneɣseɣ-as i ssut,  maca ur

yessuref Rebbi. Kkreɣ s temɣawla, senseɣ tiliẓri-nni. Sakin

yakk  tifekkiwin-nsen.  Dɣa  sardeɣ  yakk  tafekka-inu  s 
ssabun.  Sakin  slaleɣ  taserwalt-inu  akken  ad  kkseɣ  rriḥa-
nni n ẓẓel i ilesqen deg-i, tezmer ad iyi-tessenz. Uɣaleɣ ɣer 
usalun, steɣfreɣ Rebbi, sutreɣ deg-s ad yessuref lɣelṭa-inu. 
Ddmeɣ  nnesxa,  bdiɣ  taɣuri.  Maca  tugna  n  tmeṭṭut-nni

amelɛun.  Ɣas  akken,  teqqim  tugna-nni  gar  wallen-iw,  ad

i  tikkelt  niḍen.  Ur  trewwu    ara  tmeṭṭut-agi  seg  wuqu ?

uḥeččun,  ma  d  wis  sin  seg  uqerqur.  Ad  yenɛel  Rebbi

Sem, 17 seg yulyu 
 
Seg  yiḍ-nni,  tbeddel  tmuɣli-inu  ɣef  tlawin.  Uɣalent 
wallen-iw  fellunt  iselsa-nsent,    sugunent  talɣa  n  tfekka-

wakken yumeṛ tameṭṭut yumnen s tlusi n lḥiǧab akken ur 
tǧebbed  ara  tafekka-ines 
lwelha  n  urgaz.  Ugur-inu 
yennerna seg wasmi d-tuɣal uletma s axxam deg yimuras

ifrawanen  d  iwezzlanen  i  tettlusu ;  tuyat-is  d  yiḍarren-is 
ttɣimin  ɛeryan.  Tseḍḥiɣ  ad  muqleɣ  ɣur-s  neɣ  ad  qqimeɣ

anamek.  Imi  qabel  ad  ɛiwdeɣ  i  useggas,  ayɣer  ad  seɛyuɣ

is  akken  ad  ɣreɣ  akken  ilaq.  Maca  ssebba  n  ṣṣeḥ :  uɣaleɣ

ttnadiɣ  deg  yidlisen  n  lfiqh  ɣef  waddud  n  usɣan  seg

aberkan aɣezzfan, ad t-mecḍent umbaɛd ma ad t-ssuffɣen 
seg lḥebs n lximar i iɣummen iqerra-nsent s ṭul n useggas. 
Tugna-agi n tlawin, turez-iyi ɣur-s, qqureɣ kan, ula d ssut 
n  yemma  i  yi-yessawalen  ur  as-sliɣ  ara,  armi  i  yi-teqqes 
temɣart-nni  yessefraken 
lḥemmam  deg  umayeg-inu, 
tɛeggeḍ  fell-i.  Sakin,  mi  ddmeɣ  tabalizt  qesdeɣ  tawwurt 
ad  ffɣeɣ,  sliɣ-as  thedder  i  tmeṭṭut  niḍen,  tenna-as : 
« Imecṭaḥ-agi  d  ccwaṭen,  mazal  ur  ffiɣen  ara  seg  lqaɛa, 
maca allen-nsen d allen n yirgazen. Acḥal d abrid i gguleɣ 
ur  ttaǧǧaɣ  yiwen  n  umecṭuḥ  ad  yezger  amnar,  maca  ɣas 
akken  tettuɣ  iman-iw,  ttaǧǧaɣ-ten  ad  kecmen ».  Ula  d 
nekk  teqqim  tugna-nni  teṭṭafar  deg-i  acḥal  n  wussan,  d

nettat i yessakin ccehwa n tfekka-inu, dɣa uɣaleɣ ḥebbkeɣ

xeddmeɣ. Deg tallit-nni, tamussni-inu deg usɣan ur tɛeddi 
ara  almad  n  kra  n  tsurtin  n  Leqran.  Ula  d  Sidi  Lmulud, 
aselmad  n  Leqran,  ihedder-aɣ  kan  ɣef  yisental  yerzan 
almad  n  tefyar  d  tsurtin,  ur  yuɣ  ara  tannumi  yettmeslay 
yid-neɣ  s  waṭas.  Yeqqar-aɣ-d  kan  uqbel  ma  nekker  ad 
neffeɣ  sɣur-s,  ilaq  ad  naɣ  awal  i  yimawlan-nneɣ,  ad 
nbaɛɛed ɣef tkerkas d tkerḍa. Tuẓulin-a qqiment deg-i. Ur

ulamma ḥwajeɣ neɣ yettawwi-iyi ṭṭmeɛ. Deg tallit-nni llan 
« yixammen  imeqqranen »  deg  tuget  n  temdinin.  Ma 
iḥulfa yilemẓi i tfekka-ines tebɣa ad tmass tameṭṭut, abrid 
yettawin  ɣer  tullas  n  « uxxam  n  tquḥbit »  yeshel  i  tifin. 
Cfiɣ  mliḥ  ɣef  tikkeklt  tamezwarut  ideg  ṭṭseɣ  akked 
tmeṭṭut.  D  ameddakkel-iw  Lǧilali  i  yi-yewwin  ɣer  din. 
Lliɣ  deg  uɣerbaz  n  usileɣ  n  yiselmaden  deg  Xmis 
Melyana, sɛiɣ snat n tmerwin n yiseggasen, jehdeɣ, aglim-
inu imal mliḥ ɣer tebrek, kemmlen-as yinẓaḍen n cclaɣem 
d  tamart,  ɣef  waya  lliɣ  ttbineɣ-d  meqqreɣ  ugar.  Kukraɣ 
ciṭuḥ  mi  kecmeɣ  ɣer  ubraḥ  ahrawan  yeččuren  s  tid 
yesnuzuyen tayri, yal yiwet tefser tafekka-ines tahuskayt, 
maca tabɣest n Lǧilali, i ifernen tameṭṭut i yiman-is, yerna 
tayeḍ i nekk, tsellek-iyi. Ḍefreɣ tameṭṭut-nni ɣer texxamt-
is,  xeddmeɣ  iwumi  zemreɣ  akken  ad  snejliɣ  akukru-nni. 
Temdel  kan  tawwurt,  tenna :  « Yallah,  kkes  aserwal-ik ».

yekres  mačči  d  kra.  Ussan-nni,  lliɣ  xeddmeɣ  deg  tnarit  n 
Si Nasser uqbel ma ad ldiɣ tanarit-inu. Xedmeɣ yid-s ugar 
n seddis n yiseggasen. Ass-nni d tikkelt tamezwarut ideg

sent, ɣas akken ddreɣ tallit n tegrawla. Mi ara d-yekcem s 
axxam,  yettuɣal-d  s  wurfan.  Kra  n  wussan  umbaɛd, 
kecmen  yirgazen  n  tɣellist  taserdasant  s  axxam-nneɣ  deg 
yiḍ,  wwin  mmi.  Qrib  i  mmuteɣ  deg  wussan-nni,  qellbeɣ 
fell-as  deg  lkumisaryat  n  temsulta,  ɣer  temsetla,  qqaren-
iyi-d  irkelli  ulac  acu  ẓran  fell-as.  Nnan-iyi-d  kra  ahat  d 
tarbaɛt  n  yineḍliben  i  t-yewwin  ɣef  temsal  yerzan 
tanezzut  n  sselɛa  yettwagedlen.  Ṭṭfen-t  ɣur-sen  ugar  n 
waggur.  Mi  s-serḥen,  yuɣal  s  axxam,  qrib  ur  t-taɛqil  ara 
imi  aṭas  i  ibeddel.  Ɣlint-as  snat  n  tuɣmas    seg  wuglan 
unnigen,  iselsa-ines  rkan,  qersen  irkelli.  Yuɣal-aɣ-d  d 
imirqiq am usɣar. Yeqqim deg uxxam, ur yeffiɣ ara irkelli 
acḥal n wagguren, yezga ireggem, yettgalla ad d-yerr ttar. 
Yugi  ad  ɣ-yales  d  acu  s-yeḍran  deg  lḥebs.  Maca  mi  ara 
nwali  ddɣel  i  yesɛa  mgal  yal  yiwen  yesɛan  assaɣ  d 
unagraw  n  Bumedyen,  ad  neḥsu  kksen  fell-as  sser, 
sbehdlen-t, sɛeddan-t deg ssikkis, Fransa ur t-tesɛeddi ara 
ɣef  Yizzayriyen.  Yenna-as  ɛemmi-s  ad  yinig  ɣer  umkan 
niḍen  ibaɛden  ideg  ulac  win  i  t-yessnen,  wa  ad  yeḥbes 
tirdayin-ines,  acku  Bumedyen  d  anezmar,  ɣur-s 
imjelkaḍen  teqqur  tasa-nsen.  Tikkelt-a,  yezmer  ur  itteffeɣ 
seg bu-yikurdan-nsen, ḥala ma yuɣal d tafekka taqqurant, 
neɣ  d  amaɛḍur  ur  yezmir  ara  ad  yelḥu.  Iɣab  mmi  kra  n

  Lezzayer n Bumedyen mačči d Lezzayer n tegrawliyin

aḥric seg tfekka-ines yeqreḥ-it : ssker, tussda n yidammen,

ttzuruɣ-t  yal  mi  ara  sɛuɣ    ccɣel  deg  Blida  ideg  yezdeɣ

ayɣer i yefren Blida ? Yenna : « Tebɣiḍ ad meḍleɣ iman-iw 
akked twacult-iw deg tlemmast n yifri n ujrad anda luleɣ ? 
Jerbeɣ ssehra d tsila n ufella, ad k-d-iniɣ tidet, tudert berra 
n  temdinin  n  ugafa  tewɛer,  yernu  ur  tesɛi  ara  lbenna.

yeḥdeq,  ur  fhimeɣ  ara  ayɣer  i  t-ḥebsen.  Ahat  mi  ibedd 
mgal  aselway  amaynut  i  d-wwin  seg  tmurt  n  Lmerruk. 
Sliɣ-as acḥal d abrid yekkat deg-s deg temsirin-ines, yenna 
fell-as d yiwen seg yizduklalen iqdimen, wid i t-yessersen 
ɣef ukersi d imakaren d imesfesden. Nekk, ur t-ssineɣ ara, 
urǧin  sliɣ  s  yisem-is.  Yettales  baba  i  yismawen  n  kra  n 
yizduklanen, maca isem-a urǧin i iɛedda ɣef umeẓẓuɣ-iw. 
Ɣriɣ deg yiwen n uɣmis, d yiwen n umǧahed d ameqqran, 
d netta i yessekren ṭṭrad n teslullit, u yewwi-d timmunent 
i  tmurt.  Aṭas  n  temsal  i  nelmed  deg  temsirin  n  umezruy 
ɣef  tegrawla  n  wunbir  d  wid  yellan  ɣef  uqerruy-is. 
Mmuten irkelli d imeɣrasen, tenɣa-ten taredsa tafransisst. 
Urǧin i ɣ-d-mmeslayen yiselmaden n umezruy ɣef urgaz-
agi.  Anda  yezga  yifri-agi  anda  i  t-ufan ?  S  tidet  d  yiwen

ara.  Aṭas  n  temsal  i  ibeddlen  daxel  n  teɣremt  tasdawant. 
iɛessasen  ɣef  tewwurt  n  umraḥ.  Ilaq  ad

fell-ak ay ameddakkel-iw Ɛebdelqader, fecleɣ irkelli, teɣli

a yessewḥacen. Ṭṭfeɣ iman-iw, sliɣ mliḥ i yiseqsiyen-nsen

ɣef usunded n yinelmaden d yisem n ukabar yellan deffir-
s. Rdan-iyi srid s uttekki ɣer ukabar n PAGS. Mi nekkreɣ,

yimdanen :  tamenɣiwt  n  ubabat  d  zzna  d  yemma-s.  Dɣa  
yerwel  ɣer  wallun  n  yimenɛulen  ideg  urǧin  yekcem  lxir. 
Lsiɣ  aselsu  n  Œdipe,  ttsuɣuɣ  tamuggit-inu  weḥd-i  kan, 
mebla  amallal.  Ur  tteffreɣ  ara  fell-ak,  deg  tfejrijt-nni 
tamenɛult  nekkreɣ  yakk  yakucen    d  yisɣanen  yellan, 
ckunṭḍeɣ  ɣer  Brumitus,  amakar  n  tmes  sɣur  yakucen  i 
yefka sakin i talsa. Sugneɣ iman-iw d Brumitus imsellek n 
talsa seg uqhar n yakucen. Maca ufiɣ amdan yettuɣal ula 
d netta d yakuc uqsiḥ, yesseɣlay lbaṭel ɣef tmital-is mi ara 
yaweḍ  ɣer  usgeld  n  udabu.  Mmektaɣ-d  tanfalit  n  Freud : 
« Imdanen  irkelli  ffɣen-d  seg  ljedra  n  uneḍlib »,  yeqsed

yeṭṭafar-it  i  lebda ?  Anamek  n  waya,  ur  nezmir  ara  ad  t-

tenɣes deg kra niḍen. Amek ad nessegzi tilin n tekriḍt deg 
tmetti  tazzayrit  deg  yal  tallit  n  umezruy-ines ?  Ulac  tallit 
ideg ulac amennuɣ, ama gar yiterrasen neɣ gar trebbuyaɛ, 
tikkwal  yettili  i  lfayda  n  kra  n  yimdanen  kan,  tikkwal  d 
amennuɣ 
tisertiyin  neɣ 
timettanin.  Ad  neqbel  ihi  s  tikti-nni  i  d-yeqqaren  takriḍt 
tella  deg  Uzzayri  seg  zik  n  zik  am  wakken  i  d-yenna 
uɣerbaz amharsan n tesleḍt n tnefsit, yettwassnen s yisem 
n  uɣerbaz  azzayri.  Nettaf  tikti-a  deg  tezrawin  i  yexdem 
deg  uzgen  amezwaru  n  uwinas  wis  mraw  d  tẓa.  Wigi  i 
yettḥuddun ɣef waddud-a bnan ifukal-nsen ɣef tumant n 
tmenɣiwin  yellan  gar  yizzayriyen,  ama  d  iɛraben  neɣ  d 
imaziɣen, i iɛeddan  ɣef uxxam  n teɣdemt.  Walan azzayri 
yessexdam  takriḍt,  tikkwal  ineqq  ɣef  yiwet  n  ssebba  i 
yezmer  ad  yefru  s  uskasi  akked  laɛqel.  Imesdurar 
ḥemmlen asexdem n lfuciwat, acku mi ara amsen yifassen-
nsen  s  yidammen  yettnerni  nnif-nsen.  Ma  wid  izedɣen 
deg  yignan,  leslaḥ  i  ḥemmlen  ad  sxedmen  s  waṭas  d 
ajenwi  i  ssufuɣen  yal  mi  ara  yili  umennuɣ.  Walan 
imejjayen-nni tuget n tfekwin yenɣan s ujenwi yellan deg 
texxamin  ideg  ttaǧǧan  lmeyytin  sedxecmen-ten  irkelli,

ttwawtent  s  waṭas  n  tiyitwin  n  ujenwi,  iswi  ihi  mačči  d

niḍen  i  yefka  uneḍlib  sɛant  iswi  niḍen,  mačči  d  aḥuddu 
ɣef  yiman  neɣ  d  asekref  n  uxsim  i  yeqseḍ,  d  asdexcem  n

tkamyunt  n  yimeḥbas  kra  n  wussan  aya.  Yeḥka-yi-d  Si 
Aḥmed,  akumisar  n  temsulta,  belli  tifekkiwin  n  yimsulta 
yettwanɣan sedxecment irkelli s rrsas d tiyitwin n ujenwi, 
ulac  acu  ara  twaliḍ  deg-sent.  Acu-t  ddɣel-agi  yellan  deg 
wulawen  n  yineḍliben-agi ?  Aserwel  n  yimeḥbas  weḥd-s 
ur  yezmir  ara  ad  yili  d  afukel  i  usdexcem  n  tfekwin  s 
tiyitwin n ujenwi. Yerra-d Frantz Fanon ɣef yimejjayen i t-
yesseɣren.  Ɣur-s  netta,  takriḍt-a  d  tiririt  ɣef  tekriḍt 
tamharsant ugar n lqern aya. Takriḍt tettarew-d takriḍt. I 
talwit tettarew-d talwit ?  Ayɣer, ijur yiwen n wass Racid 
akken ad t-magren s tekriḍt ? Tamsalt tekres ɣef waya, ur 
nezmir  ara  ad  tt-neqqen  kan  ɣer  umennuɣ  i  yettilin  gar 
yimdanen.  Ayen  yessewhamen  deg  waya,  asmi  tewwi 
Lezzayer timunnent-ines, ur ufin ara Izzayriyen anwa ara 
ɛanden  anagar  Fransa.  D  tumant  n  win  yettwaɣelben  i 
yeṭṭafaren idles d tɣerma n win i t-yernan, am wakken i d-
yeqqar Ibn-Xeldun ? Anwa i yettwaɣelben, anwa i irebḥen 
gar  Ruma  taserdasant  d  Atina  mm-tikta  d  yidles ? 
Lezzayer  tamjahedt,  tamaɣrast  akked  Fransa  mm-tatrarit 
d tikta ? Umbaɛd n tmunnent n tmurt, uzzlen yimassayen-
nneɣ imaynuten, tuget deg-sen ɣran s tefransist, ad bnun

  Uɣaleɣ-d  iḍelli  seg  yiwen  n  yinig  ukmir  i  yi-yewwin

Ɛebdelǧabar d yal yiwen seg yiɛeggalen  n twacult-is seg

amellal.  Teṭṭef-it  temsulta  deg  meɣres  yezrin,  wwin-t

yettḥaraben  ɣef  warraw-is  imecṭaḥ  mgal  yal  amihi.  Ɣef

  Yiwet n tikkelt, tessekcem-d yemma iman-is : ruḥ aɣ-d 
i uletma-k ayen teḥwaǧ. 
Nniɣ-as :  ayɣer  ur  tettruḥu    ara  nettat  s  timmad-is  akken 
ad d-taɣ ayen i as-yehwa ? 
Tenna : kečč d argaz, teshel fell-ak tuffɣa, ma d nettat … 
Nniɣ : nettat d acu-tt ? 
Tenna :  nettat  d  tameṭṭut…  tebɣiḍ  ad  twaliḍ  uletma-k 
tettawi tettarra sdat n lǧiran ? 
Nniɣ :  ayɣer  ur  thedreḍ  ara  akka  mi  tettruḥu  weḥd-s  ɣer 
yillel am urgaz, neɣ illel yebɛed ɣef wallen n lǧiran ? 
Tessusem yemma, ulac acu i yi-d-tenna. 
  Tikkelt taneggarut ideg temmeslay yid-i uletma ur as-
rriɣ  ara  awal,  tergem-iyi,  ulac  acu  i  yi-teǧǧa.  Maca  ɣas 
akken, susmeɣ, ṭṭfeɣ iles-iw. Dɣa tuɣal ula d nettat ur iyi-
d-thedder ara. Akka xir. 
  Ulac acu i as-nniɣ i baba ɣef yinig-inu. Ẓriɣ ur iḥebbes

neɣsent  seg  wasmi  kecmeɣ  ɣer  tesdawit,  maca  ussan-a 
aql-aɣ deg yimuras. D acu ad as-iniɣ ma yesseqsa-yi-d ɣef 
tnila n yinig-inu, yernu ẓriɣ ad iyi-yesseqsi ? Nniɣ-as kan i

yemma-s, mebla ifutas. Mi iyi-yesseqsa sani leḥḥuɣ, nniɣ-

Rebbi ad iyi-yeḥrez wa ad yili yid-i deg yinig-inu. 
 
Inig yeḍra-d  deg  yiḍ. Teqleɛ  yis-neɣ lkar ɣer  lmeɣreb, 
abrid  srid  ɣer  unẓul.  Tegla-d  yemma-s  n  Ɛebdelǧabar  s 
snat n tqeftin annect ilatent, ẓẓayit mačči d kra. Faqeɣ, seg 
tazwara,  ččurent  s  yal  ssenf  n  wučči  d  yiselsa.  Yiwet 
tewwi-tt  i  mmi-s  ameḥbus,  ma  d  tayeḍ  thegga-aɣ-tt-id  i 
nekkni,  deg-s  akk  ayen  i  yettcedhi  wul  n  umessikel.  D 
tikkelt  tamezwarut  i  walaɣ  xalti  Yamina.  D  tameṭṭut  d 
tazurant,  d  talemmast  deg  lqedd,  telsa  yiwen  n  lḥiǧab  d 
aqehwi,  terra  ɣef  wudem-is  yiwen  n  laɛǧar  d  amellal. 
Tessenmer-aɣ aṭas, tedɛa-aɣ s teɣzi n laɛmer mi neqbel ad 
tt-nsaɛef  deg  yinig-agi  ukmir.  Lkar 
teččur  s 
yimessukal, tuget deg-sen  seg  unẓul,  ttwaɛeqlen  s uglim-

tikli.  Tessaɛya-ten  tmanaɣt  s  zzhir  d  wuguren-ines.  Ma  d

Yeḍɛef  mliḥ,  iban-iyi-d  am  wakken  yennerna  deg  lqedd. 
Ur  teḥbis  ara  yemma-s  seg  yiseqsiyen  ɣef  tudert-is  deg 
umkan-a,  ɣef  wučči  i  itett,  twehha-as-d  sakin  ɣef  tqufet  i 
as-d-tewwi,  tebda  la  s-tḥesseb  deg  lesnaf  n  wučči  i  as-d-
tewwi.  Ma  d  Ɛebdelǧabar,  yeqqim  kan  yettɛawad  bxir  i 
yella, ulac acu i t-ixussen anagar imawlan d yimeddukkal. 
Yeḥka-as s tewzel ɣef uneqqel-ines seg lkazirna ɣer tayeḍ, 
seg tkamyunt ɣer tayeḍ, uqbel ma t-rren daxel n yiwen n 
usafag  aserdasan  i  t-yewwin  srid  ɣer  sseḥra.  Ulac  deg 
yimeslayen-is later n tuzzma, n usḥissef neɣ n kra n ddɣel, 
yenna-d kan ayen i as-iḍerrun d lebla i d-yekkan sɣur Sidi 
Rebbi  akken  ad  ijerreb  lɛibad-is  yumnen  yis-s  d  wid 
yettḥuddun ɣef usɣan-ines. 
  Tirza-nneɣ ur tɛeṭṭel ara aṭas. Umbaɛd mi nsellem fell-
as, yenna-as Yasin : 
—Ad d-nuɣal deg waggur i d-iteddun ma yebɣa Rebbi. 
  Yerra-as Ɛebdelǧabar : 
—Ur  seɛyu  ara  iman-ik  a  gma  Yasin  …  ur  nettɣimi  ara 
dagi i lebda. Aql-aɣ bxir, lḥemdu lillah, lmeḥna-nneɣ qrib 
ad tfak. Yezmer lḥal ad ɣ-serḥen deg kra n lweqt. 
  Tenna-as yemma-s s lferḥ : 

 
 
- 291 - 

 

—Ncallah a mmi … ncallah… 
  Nemfaraq  sakin.  Yuɣal  Ɛebdelǧabar  ɣer  uqiḍun-ines  s

yeddmen  taqufet,  neṭṭafar-it  s  wallen-nneɣ  almi  i  iɣab 
irkelli.  Nufa  lkar  mazal  tettraǧu  deg-neɣ  deg  uzɣal, 
anehhar-ines  yekkumec  ɣef  yijdi,  iɣum  iman-is  s  kra  n 
ubeḥnuq  ur  yekfi  ara  i  tfekka-ines  tuḍɛift.  Udmawen  n 
yimẓuren    nnecraḥen,  ilsawen-nsen  ur  ḥbisen  ara  seg 
umeslay.  Yettwakkes  fell-asen  lhemm  i  yesberken  ussan-

iɛeggalen n twaculin-nsen i yettraǧun tuɣalin-nsen s lxuf, 
uggaden ad d-uɣalen ɣur-sen s yir lexbar.

ɣer tmersit n temdint, sakin neṭṭef lkar n yiḍ i yettawin ɣer 
Lezzayer  tamanaɣt.  Ɛyiɣ  mliḥ,  bɣiɣ  ad  ṭṭseɣ.  Ǧǧiɣ  Yasin 
yettawi yettara deg umeslay d tin ara yuɣalen d taḍeggalt-
is, ma d nekk tewwi-yi tnafa. 
 
Serseɣ  tazmamt  n  Nabil.  D  wigi  d  isebtar  ineggura

tikkelt  niḍen,  ḥekkreɣ  mliḥ  deg  yisebtar  yettucergen. 
Anwa  i  ten-icerrgen ?  Cergen-ten,  acku  ččuren  s  yisallen

—Kečč  d  amastan,  teẓriḍ  axir-iw  amek  leḥḥun  yimeẓla  n

ttesriḥ  sɣur  n  uwkil  n  tegduda.  Ur  nezmir  ara  daɣen  ad

—Ad  d-irandi  kan  i  teɣdemt,  axir-as.  Qenneɛ-it  s  waya. 
Win irewlen seg lḥebs, ulac azref i yesɛa, kulci ibedd deg
