n  teqsiḍt-inu.  Imeslayen  imezwura  ulɣen  ɣef  yiles-iw, 
maca  ɣas  akken  ulac  acu  xedmeɣ,  susmeɣ.  Tella  yiwet  n 
taɣect  i  d-yeffɣen  seg  daxel-iw,  tbedd  deg  wudem-iw. 
Ayɣer  ad  ḍeggreɣ  iman-iw  ɣer  umdun  yeččuren  s 
yizerman ?  I  wakken  ur  ttqirriɣ  ara  s  wuffir-inu,  beddeɣ, 
nniɣ-as  ad  ruḥeɣ  s  abduz.  Mi  d-uɣaleɣ,  ufiɣ  Si  Aḥmed 
ibedd  yettmeslay  d  bab  n  usečču,  xelseɣ  ayen  nečča, 
neffeɣ. 
  Uqbel  n  lmeɣreb,  uɣaleɣ  ɣer  ssbiṭar.  Ruḥeɣ  srid  ɣer 
tesga  n  usaki  ad  waliɣ  sani  tewweḍ  liḥala  n  tmeṭṭut  n 
Racid. Mi wwḍeɣ ɣer tawwurt n tesga, terra-yi-d yiwet n 
temɣart ɣer deffir, d timsizdegt, tella tetsiyiq agens.  
—Iɛedda  wakud  n  tirza  a  Si  Muḥemmed…  eǧǧ-iyi  ad 
seyqeɣ  amkan  deg 
lɣerḍ-iw…  agens  yezga  yumes, 
tettawim  tettaram  dagi,  issebbaḍen-nwen  ččuren  d  aluḍ 
neɣ  d  akal,  u  anemhal  yezga  yekkat  deg-nteɣ  belli  d 
nekkenti ur nxeddem ara ccɣel-nteɣ… 
  Uɣaleɣ srid ɣer ṭumubil-inu. Racid, ulac-it. Ad ruḥeɣ s 
axxam-is ad nadiɣ fell-as. 
 
 

 
 
- 308 - 

 
 
 

 

- 11 - 

 
 
  Mazal ur kcimeɣ ara ɣer tnarit-inu, armi i yi-d-tmuger 
tneflust-inu s usali uqsiḥ : 
—Tesliḍ s usali a « ustad » ? 
  Brarḥent  wallen-iw,  qqimeɣ 
ttmuquleɣ  kan  deg 
yicenfiren-is, ttraǧuɣ melmi ad td-enṭeq wa ad iyi-d-tini d 
acu-tt twaɣit-agi tamaynut yeḍran. 
—Akumisar n temsulta… nɣan-t tasebḥit-a sdat n uxxam-
is. 
—Si Aḥmed … d awezɣi … anwa i am-d-yennan akka ? 
—Akka i heddren akk medden… tameddakkelt-iw tezdeɣ 
deg  yiwen  n  uzaduɣ  ur  nebɛid  ara  ɣef  win  ideg  yezdeɣ 
ukumisar.  Txeddem  d  tanawart  deg  umeẓlu  n  tebzert. 
Tura  kan  i  tt-id-mugreɣ  deg  ubrid,  tleḥḥu  s  axeddim-is. 
Mazal ur as-yekkis ara lfeqɛa. Tenna-yi-d tesla i tiyitwin n 
rrsas seg uxxam-is. D tikkelt tamezwarut ideg tesla i ssut n 
rrsas sdat-s. Mi tella thedder yid-i, teqqim tettwali kan ɣer 
tama  tayeffust  d  tama  taẓelmaḍt.  Tenna-yi-d  d  at-
yiččumar i t-yenɣan. Nettat ulac acu twala. Maca aṭas seg 
lǧiran-is  walan  irebraben  seg  ṭṭwiqan  d  yibalkuten-nsen. 
Sɛan  aččamar,  lsan  iqendyar.  Win  i  ijebden  fell-as  d 
awezzlan deg lqedd, d aberkan. Tenna-yi-d temddukkelt-
iw, iwumi ibeddel wudem, yuɣal d awraɣ, tettmuqqul ɣer 

 
 
- 309 - 

 

uyeffus  d  uẓelmaḍ  seg  tuggdi,  d  yiwet  seg  tǧartin-ines  i 
as-yennan,  deg  wussan-agi  ineggura  twala  aberkan-nni 
awezzlan yeddawar  gar yizadaɣen d yiwen seg warraw n 
udcir.  Ineḍliben  ddawaren  sdat  n  tewwura-nneɣ,  nekkni 
neṭṭes,  ur  neẓri  acemma.  Nnɣan-t  d  kraḍ  seg  yiɣallen  n 
laman  daxel  n  ṭumubil,  ukren-asen  leslaḥ,  rewlen.  Anwa 
ad aɣ-iḥudden, imi tamsulta s timmad-is ur tezmir ara ad 
tḥudd ɣef yiman-is ? 
  Tamayt  i  Yakuc,  lḥamdulillah  imi  baba  d  watmanten-
iw  ur  llin  ara  d  imsulta.  Deg  waggur  yezrin  nɣan  yiwen 
deg ssuq n « Miksik », deg ddurt iɛeddan nɣan seddis deg 
ṭṭerf  n  temdint  …  ad  yester  Rebbi  tameddit  …  wigini 
teḍra-asen  am  lmektub,  ulac  win  i  izemren  ad  ibedd  deg 
wudem-sen, neɣ  ad asen-yerwel… 
 
Feqɛeɣ mačči d kra, yekref yiles-iw, ur ssawḍeɣ ara ad 
d-suffɣeɣ  ula  d  yiwen  n  wawal.  Ǧǧiɣ  taneflust-inu 
tessuffuɣ tuggdi izedɣen ul-is, kecmeɣ ɣer tnarit-inu. Rriɣ 
deg uqerruy-iw, i kra n lweqt kan, tiwlifin n temlilit-nneɣ 
n  yiḍelli.  Mazal  ttwaliɣ  Si  Aḥmed  lmendad-iw  itett  u 
yettmeslay  s  yiwet  n  taɣect  tazurant.  Subḥanllah  i 
yettbeddilen  kulci  deg  yiwen  n  wass.  Iḍelli  kan  tuɣ-it 
yedder,  yettheggi  isenfaren  i  yimal-ines ;  ass-a  yuɣal  d 
tafekka taqqurant, ad yeẓẓel snat n lmitrat ddaw n wakal, 
ad  yuɣal  d  učči  i  yiwekkiwen,  ula  d  imdanen  ad  ččen 
aksum-is. 
 
Serseɣ  iman-iw  ɣer  wattag,  tiwlifin  n  yiḍelli  mazal-
itent  ttemyeckaḍent  deg  wallaɣ-iw.  Isallen  yessefqaɛen 
ɣellin-d  fell-i  d  tirni.  Tuggdi  n  tneflust-inu  tesɛa  llsas : 

 
 
- 310 - 

 

anwa  ad  aɣ-iḥudden,  imi  temsulta  s  timmad-is  ur  tezmir 
ara ad tḥudd ɣef yiman-is ? D wigi ihi mraw n yiseggasen 
n tmettant d uhuddu i aɣ-yettraǧun umbaɛd mi nesɛedda 
mraw n yiseggasen n « i tudert yelhan » i jeggren s lbanan

Nabil s tersast ur neẓri ara amek i tewweḍ ɣer tfekka-ines 
tuḍɛift. D tinɣiman s tidet am wakken i d-nnan yimejjayen 
i walan tafekka-ines ? Neɣ yella wuffir ur neẓri ara d acu-

ideg ttwanɣan seddis n yimdanen. Nekk s timmad-iw ufiɣ 
iman-iw leḥḥuɣ deg tlemmast n yiḍ, zzuɣuren-iyi ɣer yifri 
n  yimnafqen,  selleɣ  i  wayen  ur  yeettamen  laɛqel.  Uɣaleɣ

nettwali  ḥala  deg  ssinima,  teɛna  kan  timura  niḍen  baɛdit 
fell-aneɣ.  Tura  ur  lliɣ  ara  d  imferreǧ  kan  am  wakken  lliɣ 
zik-nni, qqimeɣ ɣer deffir  ttaḍsaɣ  ɣef  lemḥayen n wiyaḍ, 
skerkren-iyi  mebla  lebɣi-inu  ɣer  wannar  n  umennuɣ, 
amek ad tili taggara-inu. Ad yester Rebbi tameddit. Hatta 
ula  d  Nasira  tesreɛ,  yezmer  lḥal  urǧin  ad  d-taki,  ad  teǧǧ 
argaz-is  weḥd-s,  d  uḥzin,  ur  yeẓri  d  acu  ad  yexdem  mi 
yewweḍ ɣer tmeddit n tudert-is. Ẓureɣ-t iḍelli deg uxxam-
is.  Ufiɣ-t  yeḥzen,  yuyes.  Ruḥeɣ  ad  t-wasiɣ  s  umeslay  ɣef 
kra n yisental bɣiɣ ad ilin baɛdit ɣef leḥzen, maca yewhem 
deg-i, tikkwal yettara-yi-d s tsusmi, tikkwal niḍen yettara-
yi-d s kra n tenfaliyin ur qqinent ara maḍi ɣer usentel i d-
wwiɣ. Ziɣ ur iyi-isell ara maḍi, yella ihedder kan i yiman-

bniɣ  fell-as,  yeṭṭerḍeq  d  imeṭṭwen.  Ssut-is  qrib  ad  yeffeɣ

ɣer berra. Ugar n yimeṭṭawen i  igezzmen  tasa-w,  yekcem

- 312 - 

 

  Deg  yiḍ  yezrin  ur  ṭṭiseɣ  ara  mliḥ.  Ɛawaz,  qqimeɣ

yezrin fell-i.  
—A « ustad » … a « ustad »... 
  Refdeɣ aqerruy-iw ɣer tneflust. Tbedd luhi n lmitra ɣef 
wattagen, ɣef yiɣallen-is aɛemmur n tewriqin. 
—Ɣur-k ass-a yiwet n tbeddi deg uxxam n teɣdemt. 
  Muqleɣ  ɣur-s,  snemmreɣ-tt,  ssutreɣ  deg-s  sakin  ad 
tessers akaram-nni ɣef tnarit. 
  Walaɣ ssaɛa yettuɛelqen deg lḥiḍ. Tesɛa u rrbeɛ. Ttuɣ

amgared  yellan  gar  bab  n  yiwen  n  uxxam  d  aqdim  d 
yiwen  n  ukerray  i  yugin  ad  as-ixelles  lekra  acku  aṭas  i 
yesref fell-as mi yekker ad t-iseggem. Dɣa iwekkel-iyi bab 
n uxxam akken ad as-d-awiɣ izerfan-is. Lethaɣ s wuguren 
i  yi-yeḍran,  ttuɣ  ad  ɣreɣ  akken  iwata  akaram-a.  Ad 
ssutreɣ  awexxer.  Mačči  d  tamsalt  iḥaren.  Nezmer  daɣen 
ad d-naf amtawi mebla ma nɛedda ɣef unezzarfu. 
  Walaɣ imidawen-inu imastanen deg umraḥ n uxxam n 
teɣdemt,  llan  deg  kraḍ  yid-sen,  ttqessiren  s  laɛqel  kan,

ḥezneɣ,  maca  ur  iyi-terri  ara  tmara  ad  sbeggneɣ  leḥzen-

wudem usrid. Ur ḥezzneɣ ara ɣef medden irkelli. Ma ulac

imidaw-nneɣ  s  usqecmeɛ,  acku  yezga 
yettawi-d isallen imaynuten. 
—Tesliḍ s usali ? 
—Ih… sliɣ yis-s… iḍelli kan i lliɣ d umerḥum deg usečču

aneggaru  akken  ad  t-tawi  s  axeddim-ines.  Nnan-d  kra  n 
yinigan, mi teffeɣ kan ṭumubil-nni gar yizaduɣen, ffɣen-d 
sin n yirgazen llan daxel n yiwet n ṭumubil i iḥebsen deffir 
n  uzaduɣ  i  ten-iqablen.  Ayen  yessewhamen,  ulac  win  i 
sen-ifaqen. Yiwen deg-sen yesɛa yiwet n lmitrayet n ssenf 
n  kalacnikuf,  ixaḍ  ṭumubil-nni  s  tersasin.  Ibedd  sdat  n 
ṭumubil, ur ssawḍen ad xedmen kra. Mmuten imir-n kan. 
Uẓan  sin  n  yineḍliben-nni  ɣur-sen,  ldin  tiwwura  n 
ṭumubil, wwin yakk leslaḥ. Sakin, rewlen s ṭumubil-nsen, 
ulac win yeẓran sani. 

 
 
- 314 - 

 

  Yesseqsa yiwen seg yimestanen : 
—Amek ad ẓeḍmen ɣef yimsulta s sshala am ta, mebla ma 
zemren ad ḥudden ɣef yiman-nsen ? 
  Yerra-as-d Buɛlam, am leɛwayed-is,  s yiwet n taɣect n 
win yessnen, yeẓran kulci. 
—D lqella n termit, d lqella n usileɣ ay ameddakkel… wali 
kan lḥeṭṭa n yimsulta-nneɣ. D izuranen, ččuren d tassemt, 
ccɣel-nsen  d  aluɛej  d  uqhar  deg  yiɣermanen.  Win  yelhan 
deg-sen  ur  yezmir  ara  ad  yeḍfer  yiwen  n  yilemẓi  yesɛan 
snat  n  tmerwin  n  yiseggasen  i  yukren  tasakuct  n  tmeṭṭut 
deg  ubrid.  Ẓewren  kan  deg  usqiqer  deg  yinehharen  n 
yiṭaksiyen  d  yimsenza  n  lxeḍra  d  lfakya,  akken  ad  asen-
kksen idrimen.

—D  wagi  i  d  ugur  n  temsulta  deg  tallit  n  talwit  d 
uskenwu. Aqhar, tameḥqranit, asemɣer n yiman d tukksa 
n  yidrimen.  « Ḥala  idɣaɣen  ara  d-yegrin  deg  wasif ». 
Yewweḍ-d  lawan  n  lemḥasba.  Win  i  tt-ixedmen,  ad  tt-
ixelles. 
—D  lɛib  a  Ssaɛid,  i  s-yenna  Buɛlam  Seɛdun.  Akumisar  d 
argaz lɛali, d uɣdim… 
—Ur  qsiḍeɣ  ara  argaz-a  beddat…  isem-is  zeddig  mliḥ… 
nekk  ttmeslayeɣ  ɣef  temsulta  s  umata.  Ɣur-wen  irkelli 
iwezla  n  yiɣermanen  yetcetkayen  ɣef  uqhar  n  yimsulta, 
neɣ ala ? 
—Yal  awal  deg  lawan-is,  ameslay  ass-a  ad  d-yawi  ɣef 
leḥzen daya kan. Bedret lmeggtin-nwen s wawal aẓiḍan. 

 
 
- 315 - 

 

—Maca ɣas akkenni  eǧǧ-iyi ad  ak-d-iniɣ  belli timsulta ur 
tɛass  ara  iman-is,  ur  tbeddel  ara  tikli-ines.  Wwten-ten 
ɛlaɣila,  ur  bnin  ara  fell-as.  Ma  nquren  Ɛayn-el-kerma  d 
temdinin  niḍen,  ad  nwali  takriḍt  ur  tt-tḥuz  ara  zik. 
Wwḍen-aɣ-d kra n yisallen d akken tuget seg wid yeffɣen

ideg  ffɣen yimjuhad  s  waṭas.  Wagi d aferdis agejdan deg 
usnerni n tekriḍt n yirebraben-a. Kesben yirebraben tirmit 
deg tmenɣiwt, ma d timsulta teqqim tezzuɣur ibriren-ines 
seg wass ɣer wayeḍ. 
—Nniɣ-as,  tesɛiḍ  lḥeqq.  Akumisar  yella  ileḥḥu  mebla 
aɛessas, mebla ma iɛass iman-is, ad as-tiniḍ mazal-aɣ deg 
yiseggasen-nni  n  telwit.  Iḍelli  kan  ufiɣ-t  ibedd  ɣer 
tewwurt  n  uxxam  n  temsulta,  yettmeslay  d  yiwen  seg 
yimidawen-ines,  iruḥ  sakin  yid-i,  weḥd-s,  ɣer  usečču, 
yernu  ula  d  tameẓyant-ines  swayes  yezmer  ad  iḥudd  ɣef 
yiman-is ur cukkeɣ ara yewwi-tt yid-s. 
  Yenna-d  umastan  amezwaru  s  yiwet  n

—D  ayen  yessewhamen,  ur  tfehmeḍ  acemma…  yal  ass 
imegger  rrsas  timerwin  n  teɣtas,  isallen  n  usedrem,  n 
uhuddu d usṭerḍeq ttaččaren isebtar n yiɣmisen, maca ɣas 
akken teqqim temsulta n Ɛayn-el-kerma tettḥewwis ad as-
tiniḍ deg tmurt n Swisra neɣ deg tmurt n Ssuwid i tella. 
i  nga  nekkni  s  yimestanen,  nḥemmel  ad 
  Akka 
nemmeslay s laɛyaḍ wa ad nerdu imdanen. Ahat mi neẓra 

taɣect 

 
 
- 316 - 

 

tiwuɣa  i  iḍerrun  deg  tmetti-nneɣ,  nuɣal  nettwali  ccer  d 
ddɣel deg yal amkan. Maca Si Aḥmed yuklal awal aẓiḍan. 
Ɣef waya skecmeɣ iman-iw, nniɣ : 
—Win ur nesɛi ara tuga deg uɛebbuḍ-is, ur yettaggad ara 
times… d tagi d liḥala n Si Aḥmed… d amsaltu d uɣdim, 
yeṭṭafar asaḍuf, ur iḥeqqer yiwen. Ur yeksib ula d yiwet n 
ṭumubil, d anza belli ur yessexdam ara tawuri-ines akken 
ad yekseb idrimen, am wakken xeddmen wiyaḍ. 
  Yenna-d Buɛlam Seɛdun : 
—Amerḥum yella d amedya deg uxeddim-ines, ad cehdeɣ 
ɣef  waya.  Beddren-t-id  ḥala  deg  lxir.  Bexlaf  wiyaḍ  i 
ijemɛen  igerrujen  deg  kra  n  yiseggasen,  ad  tɣileḍ  d  ifri  n 
Ɛli Baba i ufan. 
  Yewweḍ-d  ssut  n  umaray  neɣ  n  uneflus  n  uxxam  n 
teɣdemt  i  d-yeqqaren  yebda  yibeddi,  dɣa  nruḥ  wa  deffir 
wa ɣer tzeqqa tameqqrant. 
  Tawacult  n  Si  Aḥmed  teṭṭef  rray  ad  t-temḍel  deg 
taddart  ideg  ilul.  Taddart-nni  tameẓyant  anda  yebɣa  ad 
yesɛeddi  tastaɣt-ines  gar  umadaɣ-ines.  Aṭas  n  yimsulta 
yeddan  deg  temṭelt-ines.  Nruḥ  d  tarbaɛt.  Deg  tazwara, 
ugiɣ ad dduɣ ɣer tẓegwa-nni ideg yekkes laman. Acḥal n 
yisallen  yessewḥacen  i  aɣ-d-yettawḍen  seg  yidurar-nni 
akken  ad  aɣ-ssergigin  seg  tuggdi,  wa  ad  aɣ-gedlen 
anekcum ɣer-sen. Yeffeɣ wawal belli d timnaḍin tilelliyin, 
tḥekkem-itent  trebbuyaɛ  timselḥin,  teqher  imezdaɣ-is,  d 
imesdurar,  d  ikerrazen,  ur  sɛin  ara  assaɣ  d  umennuɣ 
iḍerrun deg tmurt. D tudrin yezgan deg yidurar, ulac deg-
sent  iɣallen  n  laman.  La  tamsulta  wala  tamsetla.  Ḥala 

 
 
- 317 - 

 

tayunin  n lɛesker i yeddawaren  tikwal dinna. Deg tilawt, 
tayunin-a  n  lɛesker  ur  nfiɛent  i  ucemma.  D  tarbaɛt 
taɣezzfant, d  taẓayant n  ṭumubilat  d yikumya yeččuren s 
lɛesker  i  sluɣmen  yiwen  n  usluɣmu  s  wudem  n  tiṭ  deg 
tallit n telwit, ur lmiden ara deg-s ulamma amek ad jebden 
s tmekḥal-nsen, ugar n waya, lemden kan tataktikt n ṭṭrad 
tamensayt. Tura mi ufan iman-nsen deg yiwen n wannar, 
udemkal-ines d idurar d tẓegwa, acengu-ines d tirebbuyaɛ 
timselḥin  yeffren  deg  yiɣeẓran,  deg  yimudaɣ,  dɣa  ad 
uɣalen  iserdasen-agi  iruḥen  ad  sɛeddin  lɛesker-nsen  d 
tiɣtas isehlen, wa ad t-nɣen s tersast, wa ad t-zlun. Mi ara 
lḥunt tɣelmin-a deg yiberdan n yidurar, ad tent-tesleḍ, wa 
ad  tent-twaliḍ  seg  mbaɛid.  Ɣef  waya  ttafen  yimnafqen 
yakk lweqt akken ad ffren iman-nsen deg yifran-nsen, ad 
rǧun kan melmi ad ɛeddin mebla ma uggaden kra. Acḥal i 
ɣriɣ deg yiɣmisen ɣef tfextin i ndin yirebraben i tɣelmin-a 
n  yiserdasen  deg  yiberdan  n  udrar  yecban  wigi,  kfant  s 
yibaxixen ad tessedḥi seg-sen talsa. 
  Mi  d-wwḍeɣ  ɣer  umraḥ  n  uzaduɣ  akked  Buɛlam 
Seɛdun,  ayen  ijebden  lwelha-w    d  amḍan n  yirgazen 
irefden leslaḥ. Meqqrit ciṭuḥ deg laɛmer, yernu iban ur llin 
seg  temsulta  neɣ  seg  temsetla  wala  seg  yiserdasen.  D 
iɣarimen  kan,  tuget  deg-sen  ṭṭfen  deg  yifassen-nsen 
timekḥal n ssyada. Usan-d deg snat n tkumya timeẓyanin 
seg  ssenf  n  « Mazda »,  am  tidak  i  ssexdamen  i  tiɣin  n 
sselɛa.  Ẓriɣ  usan-d  seg  taddart  n  Si  Aḥmed,  yiwet  n 
taddart  tameẓyant  iwumi  ssawalen  Sidi  Merzug.  Nɛezza 
sin  n  watmaten-is,  nsellem  sakin  ɣef  yal  argaz  i  d-yusan

yid-sen.  Yiwen  deg-sen  yettak  anzi  i  Si  Aḥmed,  maca 
iqewwa ciṭuḥ fell-as. Yelsa yiwet n lfista taqdimt n lɛesker, 
yessers  ɣef  uqerruy-is  yiwet  n  teɛmamt  d  tawinaɣit. 
Cclaɣem-is  ččan  udem-is,  ɣur-s  daɣen  yiwet  n  tamart  d  
tarqiqant  terna-as  tebrek  ɣef  ssifa-s.  Ɣef  tayet-is  yerfed 
yiwet  n  tmekḥelt  seg  ssenf  n  siminuf.  D  tayiwant  gar 
tmukḥal n  ssyada  iɛelqen  yirgazen ɣef tuyat-nsen.  Ibedd, 
aqerruy-is ɣer yigenni. Ur d-iban ara leḥzen ɣef wudem-is, 
am wakken i nettaf ɣef wudmawen n wid iwumi yemmut 
yiwen  seg  twacult-nsen.  Susmen  irkelli,  ṭṭafaren  kan  s 
wallen-nsen ṭumubilat i yettawin yettarran d yimɛezziyen 
i  d-yettassen.  Deg  ṭṭerf  n  umraḥ  qqimen  yirgazen  d 
yimeẓyanen  ttwalin  ayen  iḍerrun  sdat-sen  deg  tsusmi. 
Iban  d  imezdaɣ  n  yizaduɣen  niḍen  usan-d  ad  ḥeḍren  i 
usuffeɣ n tfekka n umerḥum seg uxxam-is. Ur cukkeɣ ara 
ad ddun yid-neɣ. Ruḥen-d kan ad sbeggnen ibeddi-nsen d 
twacult  n  umerḥum.  Neɣ  ahat  usan-d  kan  akka,  ur  sɛin 
ara  ccɣel  niḍen  ad  t-xedmen.  Akka  i  iga  uɣref-agi  i

wiyaḍ.    D  aferreǧ  ara  yefken  talalit  i  tmucuha  ara  ḥkun 
deg wussan d wuḍan i d-iteddun. 
 
Furseɣ  tagnit  mi  yeffreɣ  umkan  seg  yimɛezziyen

imselḥen : 
—Ansuf yis-wen … sarameɣ ur ken-yessaɛyi ara yinig… 
 
lḥemdulillah… uẓaɣ mliḥ ɣer gma-s n umerḥum : 

Sliɣ  i  kra  n  usrugmet,  fehmeɣ  kan :  labas…  walu…

Sliɣ imir-n i leswat : ad t-yerḥem Rebbi… 

—Si  Aḥmed,  d  ameddakkel-iw,  ɛziz  fell-i  mliḥ…  aṭas  i 
nettru fell-as, iɣaḍ-aɣ mačči d kra… 
  Yerra-yi-d  s  laɛqel  kan,  mebla  ma  imuqel  ɣer  wallen-
iw : 
—Ad t-yerḥem Rebbi … d lmektub n Sidi Rebbi… d tagi d 
ddunit… ɣer din i nleḥḥu irkelli… 
 
—Ur  ɛeddan  ara  sin  n  wussan  mi  iyi-d-yenna  yejjem  ad

iwala  ara  taddart-is.  Yessarem  seg  wul-is  ad  yaf  tagnit 
akken ad tt-iẓur deg wussan-a i d-iteddun. 
  Yerra-d gma-s nnehta, yenna : 
—D tamettant i as-yessawlen… akka i tḍerru d yiɣriben…

yemma-s. 
  Wehmeɣ  deg  usegzi-a,  maca  susmeɣ,  ulac  acu  i  as-
nniɣ.

u netturebba. Ahat kunwi ur teffiɣem ara seg tudrin-nwen

—D  tidet…  urǧin  ffɣeɣ  seg  taddart-iw,  akal  n  lejdud-iw, 
anagar  deg  tallit  ideg  sɛeddaɣ  lɛesker-inu.  Lliɣ  ttganiɣ 
tikci n ttesriḥ am waggur n lɛid akken ad uɣaleɣ srid ɣer 
Sidi Merzug… 
—Tella telwit deg tallit-nni… mačči am wass-a…

telwit  d  lehna.  D  tidet,  nekkni  d  igellilen,  maca  tigellelt 
urǧin  tenɣa  albaɛḍ.  Nkerrez  akal-nneɣ,  yettara-aɣ-d  lxir. 
Lliɣ  ma  serseɣ  aqerruy-iw  ɣef  tsutma,  ur  ttfiqiɣ  ara  d

deg lexla, ulac win ad t-innalen. Ɣlin-d fell-aneɣ iɛefriten-a 
ɛlaɣila,  ur  neẓri  ara  seg  wansi  i  d-usan.  Usan-d  yiwen  n

dderbuka  d  tuɣac  d  teɣratin  n  tlawin.  Newhem  deg-sen. 
Naɛreḍ-iten  i  yimensi,  ččan  sakin  hedren-aɣ.  Nniɣ-asen 
ayen yellan deg wul-iw : tamsalt-nwen ur aɣ-taɛni ara. Ma 
tesɛam  ugur  d  wat  n  Lezzayer,  ruḥet  ɣer  Lezzayer  ad  t-
tefrum.  D  acu  i  aɣ-idexlen  nekkni ?  Deg  yiḍ-nni,  ruḥen, 
nɣil dayen, tamsalt teddez tebrez. Maca uɣalen-d ɣur-neɣ, 
wwin-d  yid-sen  wiyaḍ,  aṭas  deg-sen  tikkelt-a.  Kra  n 
yilmeẓyen-nneɣ  ddan  yid-sen,  dɣa  bḍan  wat  n  Sidi

Merzug.  Maca  lbaṭel  n  wigi  iɛedda  yakk  tilisa.  Tɛeddan

nneɣ. Ass-a, ula d yiwen seg yifuḥanen-a ur yezmir ara ad 
yaẓ ɣer yixxamen-nneɣ. Ttif lmut, wala tudert n ddel. Seg 
zik  n  zik  i  nuɣ  aẓar  deg  wakal-a.  Fransa…  Fransa  s

yid-i  deg  ṭumubil-inu.  Yeqbel  s  uzmmumeg.  D  tagnit  ad

tudert  i  ssneɣ  yakan,  tura  la  tt-twaliɣ  deg  talɣa  d  tikli  n

timekḥal-nsen  ɣef  tgecrar,  rran  udmawen-nsent  ɣer  tama

—Xeddmen  tisergalin-nsen  deg  yiberdan  yettawin  ɣer

Nnan-d kra n yinigan win i t-yessuffɣen seg lkar d amdan 
i yessen mliḥ, d mmi-s n taddart-is. Mi t-iwala kan, yessers

Iḥudd  yilemẓi-nni  ɣef  yiman-is,  yenna-as    d  tamsetla  i  t-
yewwin  s  yiɣil,  tura  dayen  yekfa  lɛesker-ines,  maca  ɣas

temzelt-inek  tamezwarut  deg  lǧihad.  Nekkni  d  iserdasen

ẓriɣ  ara,  uɣaleɣ  ulac  acu  i  ẓerreɣ.  Yenneqbaḍ  wul-iw, 
ttḥulfuɣ i yiẓerman-iw qqersen daxel n tɛebbuḍt-iw. Tura 
ad kkreɣ ad waliɣ d acu zemreɣ ad xedmeɣ.

ara… Yasin yettraǧu deg-i… d acu ara as-iniɣ ?

zmireɣ ara ad qqimeɣ dagi… ur zmireɣ ara…

gar  n  tfekkiwin-nni.  Mebla  lfayda.  Dɣa  rẓiɣ  asalu  gar 
yimdanen-nni s usexdem n yiɣallen-iw akken ad awḍeɣ s 
amkan.  Tella  lḥaǧa  deg-i  i  yi-d-yeqqaren  ilaq  ad  ɣiwleɣ. 
Asayes-nni  i  walaɣ  yessewhem-iyi  mliḥ,  yerra-d  ɣer 
tidmi-w isura n lwastern i nettwali deg temẓi-nneɣ ; isura-
nni yeččuren s tfekkiwin n lmeggtin yeẓẓlen ɣef wakal neɣ 
ijdi,  ddaw  n  yiẓenẓaren  n  yiṭij  aqesḥan  n  sseḥra  n 
Kalifurnya  neɣ  Nifada.  Seddiset  n  tfekkiwin  ttuḍeggrent 
ɣef  tmurt.  Iselsa-nsent  umsent  s  wakal  d  yidammen. 
Udmawen-nsent  yečča-tent  uččamar,  jerḥent,  iban  tejhed 
tiyita  gar-asen.  Zzin-asent  yimsulta  s  yiselsa  izegzawen, 
deg yifassen-nsen ṭṭfen timekḥal, beggsen i tiyita ma yeḍra 
kra.  Ɣummen  udmawen-nsen  s  yikagulen  n  taḍuḍt 
taberkant.  Ḥala  allen-nsen  yettmecberriqen  i  yettbinen, 
ttmuqulent ɣer tama tayeffust d tẓelmaḍt, ulac acu i sent-
iruḥen, ad as-tiniḍ d lazer. Bedden ibeddi n win i yernan 
axsim-is,  iqerra-nsen  deg  yigenni,  idmaren-nsen  cuffen, 
iḍarren-nsen  rsen  ɣef  wakal  ibezgen.  Yewwet-d  ciṭuḥ  n 
ugeffur deg yiḍ. Tasebḥit-a tesfa tegnawt. Iṭij n ḥertadem 

 
 
- 351 - 

 

yessehma  amraḥ,  deg  yigenni,  anagar  kra  n  usigna  i 
yeqqimen,  yettawi-t  waḍu  ɣer  usammer.  Uẓaɣ  ɣer 
tfekkiwin,  bɣiɣ  ad  ẓreɣ  anwa-ten  wigi  yettwanɣen.  Deg 
tidmi-w  myuckaḍent  tugniwin :  Ɛebdelǧabar  s  teɣzi-ines 
d uččamar-ines aberkan yessden, mi iyi-d-ihedder daxel n 
texxamt-nni,  d  Ɛebdelḥamid  uḍɛif  mi  i  yi-yettales  i 
teqsiḍt-nni-ines  yessewhamen,  sakin  mi  ileḥḥu  nekk 
ṭṭafareɣ-t  seg  deffir  akked  Yusef  Ɛeyyaci  deg  tlemmast  n 
tebrunin  n  waman  d  waluḍ.  Xelḍent 
tugniwin  d 
yisayasen, kra usan-d seg ccfawat-inu, tiyaḍ ayen ttwalint 
wallen-iw sdat-i. 
  Udmawen-nni ttemcabin irkelli, d ixemriyen malen ɣer 
tebrek, jerḥen, ččuren s yidammen yeberguggen, akken ad 
ten-tɛeqleḍ  yessefk  fell-ak  ad  tqerbeḍ  mliḥ  ɣur-sen.  Ɣas 
akken tban-d tfekka n Ɛebdelǧabar yeẓẓlen deg tlemmast, 
tmal. Hata ihi uɣella-nni yebɣan ad yebnu anagraw aserti 
amaynut s wuzzal d tmes. Yumen s tidet yezmer ad yernu 
yiwen n udabu i ibedden azgen n lqern aya, staɛerfent yis-
s  yakk  tmura  n  umaḍal ?  Neɣ  yesderɣel-it  ddɣel,  armi 
yuɣal ur yettwali acemma anagar tiririt n ttar, d iswi-agi i 
t-yesselḥayen ? Ahat d ɛeggu akked layas seg ddunit-a i t-
yewwin  ad  iruḥ  s  yiḍarren-is  ɣer  lmut,  acku  yumen  ma 
yemmut d amḥaddi ɣef tneslemt, ad yettwaḥseb d ccahid 
neɣ d ameɣras, dɣa ad yekcem srid ɣer lǧennet ? Ayɣer ur 
as-mmeslayeɣ ara deg yiḍ-nni ɣef temsalt-a akken ad ẓreɣ 
tikta  swayes  yumen ?  Aṭas  n  temsal  nettwali-tent  kan  s 
wudem n tiṭ, ur tent-nettwali ara s telqi dɣa ur nettfiq ara 
belli ur nessin acemma fell-asent alamma iɛedda lweqt. Ur 

 
 
- 352 - 

 

ẓriɣ ara ma nezmer ad nemmeslay akka ɣef trebbuyaɛ-nni 
timeẓyanin, ur nesɛi acemma gar yifassen-nsent, maca ɣas 
akkenn  refdent  leslaḥ  deg  wudem  n  Fransa  tameqqrant ? 
Anwa  i  as-yennan  imdanen-nni  yesɛan  kan  timekḥal  n 
usegged, ad uɣalen yiwen n wass d asaḍen ihumirusiyen 
iwumi ad zzin luluf n ljunud, ad ssawḍen ad ḥettmen ɣef 
Fransa ad temcawar yid-sen, yernu ad tsemmeḥ deg yiwet 
n  tmurt  tameqqrant  am  Lezzayer  i  testaɛmer  awinas  d 
uzgen ?  I  wigi,  fkan  tudert-nsen  d  asfel  i  tmunnent  n 
tmurt-nsen ?  Neɣ  tamsalt-a  d  lemxaṭra  tatrajidit  yettawin 
kan  ɣer  sin  n  yiberdan d  inemgalen,  ulac  wis  kraḍ  : 
tarennawt  neɣ  tamettant ?  Win  yuɣen  abrid-a  yettwali 
iman-is deg yiwen n lweqt yerbeḥ, yemmut. Maca d acu i 
ten-yesselḥayen  s  tidet :  tudert  akked  trennawt  neɣ 
tamettant,  ɣas  ma  yella  ula  d  abrid-a  yettawi  ula  d  netta 
ɣer  tudert  niḍen.  Ayɣer,  tignatin-a  ttemcabint  :  tamettant 
ɣef uɣlan akked tmettant ɣef usɣan ? Zik-nni yexleḍ uɣlan 
d  usɣan ?  Medden  ttakken  tudert-nsen  d  asfel  ɣef  sin  n 
yiswan-a. Maca ass-a, aɣlan d ayla n medden irkelli, ma d 
asɣan,  tennulfa-d  tarbaɛt-a  i  yebɣan  ad  t-yerren  d  ayla-s 
nettat kan weḥd-s. Dɣa terfed leslaḥ mgal aɣlan. Yekker-d 
ihi  uɣlan-a  ad 
iḥudd  ɣef  yiman-is,  ɣef  usɣan-ines 
amezwaru  daɣen.  Iban  d  aɣlan  ara  yernun  asɣan  am 
wakken teḍra deg Yuruba. Aɣlan d ayla n medden irkelli, 
wid i t-izedɣen yakan d wid ad ikecmen ɣur-s azekka. Ma 
d asɣan yettembeddal seg wakud ɣer wayeḍ. 
  Uẓaɣ mliḥ. Bɣiɣ ad waliɣ udmawen-nni. Iqerreb-d ɣur-
i yiwen n umsaltu, udem-is iɣumm, ad as-tiniḍ yella acu i 

 
 
- 353 - 

 

yeggad.  Maca  ulac  acu  i  d-yenna.  Muqleɣ-t,  nniɣ-as  s 
yifassen-iw ulac acu ara yaggad seg tama-w, beddeɣ sakin 
sdat  n  yiwet  n  tfekka  tawezzlant  tumes  s  yidammen  d 
wakal,  tettuḍegger  ɣer  tama  tayeffust,  qrib  ad  tenṭeḍ  ɣer 
tfekka niḍen. Aqerruy-is yečča tiyita, ad as-tiniḍ s tɣawsa 
tuqḍiɛt  i  yettwawet.  Kniɣ  ɣur-s  mliḥ.  Aglim-is  imal  ɣer 
tebrek.  D  Yasin  akeḥluc ?  Win  yenɣan  Nabil ?  Asali  n 
tmenɣiwt-ines  ad  yessenɣes  seg  ddɣel  d  leḥzen  n  Racid, 
ahat  ad  as-tekkes  seg  wallaɣ-is  tikti  n  urfad  n  leslaḥ  i 
itezzin deg uqerruy-is ussan-a ineggura ? 
  Hata  tẓeḍem-d  yiwet  n  tmeṭṭut  ɣef  uqusis-nni    uḍyiq, 
tettsuɣu : mmi Yusef… Yusef mmi… 
  Tḍegger-iyi  ɣer  ṭṭerf,  tḥuza-yi,  qrib  i  yi-tesseɣli  ɣef 
tmurt.  Ɛeqleɣ-tt  s  sshala  s  lḥiǧab-ines  awinaɣ.  D  acu 
txeddem dagi yemma-s n Yusef Ɛeyyaci ? Ayɣer i tessawal 
s yisem n mmi-s am wakken deg tlemmast n tfekkiwin-a i 
yella ?  Walaɣ-tt  sakin  temmeɣ  ɣef  yiwet  n  tfekka, 
tettsuɣu :  nɣan  mmi  Yusef…  nɣan  mmi  Yusef…  Ula 
yiwen  seg  yimsulta  ur  yembawel  ara.  Bedden  qquren. 
Kerfen. Walaɣ lewhama d tuggdi ɣef wudmawen n wid i 
yezzin i umkan,  rran  lwelha-nsen irkelli  ɣer tmeṭṭut-nni  i 
yekkaten agejdur. Qrib i ttuɣ d akken Yusef yella yettiddir 
akked  terbaɛt-agi.  Mazal  ur  irandi  ara  i  temsulta ?  Ayɣer 
ur  d-yuɣal  ara  ɣur-i ?  Ugin-as  yimeddakkel-is  ad  irandi ? 
Grarbent  fell-i  tuttriwin,  ur  sent-ufiɣ  ara  ula  d  yiwet  n 
tririt.  Qqimeɣ  qqureɣ  deg  umkan-iw,  ttwaliɣ  kan  deg 
tmeṭṭut-nni  tameɣbunt.  Hata  mmi-s  ayiwan  yemmut  s 
tersasin  am  wakken  yemmut  baba-s  mraw  n  yiseggasen 

 
 
- 354 - 

 

aya.  D  mmi-s  s  tidet ?  Ahat  teɣleḍ,  temmeɣ  ɣef  tfekka 
niḍen. Maca ur tezmir ara tyemmat ad takez mmi-s ? Uẓaɣ 
ɣur-s  s  laɛqel,  ɛerḍeɣ  ad  tt-sbaɛdeɣ  ɣef  tfekka-nni. 
Tmuqel-iyi-d  s  yiwen  n  wudem  teffeɣ-it  tudert,  yejmeɛ 
i  yeɣlin  ɣef  talsa.  Taɛqel-iyi, 
weḥd-s  yakk  tiwuɣa 
teckunṭeḍ deg ubalṭu-inu, tsuɣ : 
—Nɣan-t a Si Ɛebdelqader… nɣan-t… 
—Hedden iman-im a uletma… ahat mačči d netta… 
—Muqel-it  mliḥ…  kečč  tessneḍ-t…  muqel…  mačči  d 
Yusef mmi ? 
  Refdeɣ iman-iw ciṭuḥ ɣef tfekka. D netta s tidet. Ul ac 
acu yuɣen udem-is, ur yejriḥ ara. Ciṭuḥ n wakal kan. Maca 
idmaren-is  umsen  s  yidammen  d  wakal  d  yibeɛɛayen. 
Ahat  ḥuzan-t  s  tersasin  deg  yidmaren.  Tenna-yi-d  deg 
tlemmast n yimeṭṭawen : 
—Yusa-d ɣur-i snat n ledwar aya… yenna-yi-d : azekka ad 
ruḥeɣ  ɣer  yimsulta,  ad  randiɣ…  d  acu  i  ixeddem  dagi, 
yemmut ?  Mačči  gar  yifassen  n  yimsulta  i  ilaq  ad  yili 
tura ? 
  Tḍegger  iman-is  i  tikkelt  niḍen  ɣef  tfekka  n  mmi-s  s 
yimeṭṭawen.  Heggaɣ  iman-iw  ad  knuɣ  akken  ad  tt-
sbaɛdeɣ ɣef umkan-nni. Kukraɣ ciṭuḥ,  d acu ara  as-iniɣ ? 
Tawaɣit-ines d anu ur nesɛi lqaɛ.Walaɣ liḥala-a yakan deg 
Racid  d  Nasira.  Imeslayen  weḥd-sen  ur  zmiren  ara  ad 
snejlin  leḥzen.  D  acu  ad  d-tiniḍ  i  tyemmat  iwumi  nɣan 
mmi-s.  Nɣan-t,  ḍeggren-t  deg  tlemmast  n  umraḥ  azayez 
am uneḍlib i tessusef tmetti asmi yedder d wasmi yemmut 

 
 
- 355 - 

 

daɣen ? Nettat i yumnen, yernu s tidet,  d akken ulac acu 
yexdem, d ameslan i yella, yezmer ad yemneɛ. 
  Kra n lweqt umbaɛd, ruḥen-d  sin n yimestal sbaɛden-
tt.  Tbedd,  ur  ten-teǧǧi  ara  ad  tt-sbaɛden,  tennuɣ  yid-sen 
armi  tefsex.  Usan-d  sakin  yisexsiyen,  refden-tt,  wwin-tt 
ɣer tkerrust-nsen. 
  Ula  d  nekk  ččiɣ  tiyita,  ḥezneɣ.  Ur  nwiɣ  ara  ad  d-afeɣ 
Yusef Ɛeyyaci gar teɣtas-nni. Ḥala netta i yellan d ameslan 
gar  lmeggtin-nni.  Ayɣer  ur  iruḥ  ara  ɣer  temsulta  am 
wakken  i  d-tenna  yemma-s ?  Ahat  ass-nni  i  yenwa  ad 
irandi  deg-s,  yeɣli-d  d  wass-nni  ideg  nɣan  akumisar  n 
temsulta ?  Snat  n  ledwar  yezrin  tura  ɣef  tedyant-nni 
daɣen. Tamenɣiwt n wass-nni tekkes seg uqerruy-is tikti n 
urandi ? Neɣ d ameddakkel-is Ɛebdelḥamid i t-iqenɛen ad 
yeqqim  deg  terbaɛt ?  Neɣ  ahat  yuggez-it  ad  t-ineɣ  ma 
yexdem-itt ?  Anwa  i  yeẓran ?  Neɣ  yerrunda  i  temsulta, 
dɣa ḥettmen fell-as ad yemɛawan yid-sen wa ad asen-imel 
anda  yella  umkan  ideg  ffren  yimeddukkal-is,  din  i 
yettwawet s tersasin i t-yenɣan ? Umbaɛd mi sliɣ i teqsiḍt-
nni  n  uḥeddad  d  sin  n  yimsulta  imakaren,  zemreɣ  ad 
qebleɣ  yakk  turdiwin.  Ṭṭrad-a  ifuḥ,  yumes,  ad  d-yefk 
talalit  i  kra  n  rrwayeḥ  d  tifuḥanin  i  iqebbren  ulawen,  wa 
ad  qqiment  ttafgent  deg  walun,  fellunt  deg  wulawen,  ur 
aɣ-ttaǧǧant ara ad nqabel tidet tafuḥant. 
  Yemmut  Yusef  Ɛeyyaci,  ula  d  uffir-ines  yettwamḍel 
yid-s,  am  wakken  yettwamḍel  uffir  n  Ɛebdelkrim 
aḥeddad. 

 
 
- 356 - 

 

  Kra  n  lweqt  umbaɛd  mi  wwin  yemma-s  n  Yusef  ɣer 
tkerrust  n  yisexsayen,  ɣlin-d  fell-aneɣ  yimsulta  iɣummen 
udmawen-nsen,  bdan  seɛsaqen  deg 
lɣaci.  Reffden 
tifekkiwin, ḍeggren-tent daxel n tkamyunt i ibedden tama 
n  usebdad  n  yimeɣrasen.  Nnejmaɛen  sakin  deg  tlemmast 
n umraḥ, bdan kkaten s leslaḥ ɣer yigenni, reffden ifassen-
nsen.  Tiyita  n  rrsas  tessexleɛ  lɣaci,  dɣa  rewlen.  Uɣalen 
yimsulta-nni  ɣer  ṭumubilat-nsen,  ffɣen  seg  umkan-nni  s 
yisuɣan n trennawt. 
  Ula  d  nekk  ulac  acu  ara  xedmeɣ  deg  umraḥ-nni. 
Skerkreɣ iḍarren-iw, teffeɣ-iyi tezmert, ttaɛraḍeɣ amek ad 
qeɛdeɣ 
iluɣen.  Ṭṭafaren-iyi 
wudmawen d tewlifin d yiseqsiyen i irennun deg-i reffu d 
leḥzen.  Mmektaɣ-d  ass  n  unekcum-inu  amezwaru  ɣer 
Ɛayn-el kerma, deg uqrab-iw tawerqet n tummlin-inu deg 
uɣerbaz  alemmas  « Ibn  Badis »,  ul-iw  yeččur  s  tumert, 
bɣiɣ ad ddreɣ akken ilaq, allaɣ-iw yeččur s tirga yelhan d 
yisenfaren, dɣa tmuger-iyi-d am yisli i irekben agmer i d-
yusan  ad  tt-inaseb.  Anda-tt  Ɛayn-el-kerma-nni,  anda-tt 
tamdint-nni  turkidt  ideg  tezdeɣ  talwit,  yesterḥiben  s 
yinebgawen ? Ad d-tuɣal yiwen n wass ? Melmi ?
